Thank you.</div>\n</div>\n\n\n\n\n\n<!-- FEATURED POST -->\n\n<!-- REGULAR POSTS -->\n\n\n\n    \n\n\n\n\n<!-- entry shared -->\n\n<article class="post entry">\n\n\n\n<!-- DISPLAY FULL POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/any-takers.html">Any Takers?</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a30d418201200b-pi"><img alt="DD1309F3-7AFA-4FD3-A2B9-6CF0BD533880" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202a30d418201200b img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a30d418201200b-450wi" style="width: 450px; display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="DD1309F3-7AFA-4FD3-A2B9-6CF0BD533880" /></a></p>\r\n<p>A meme says a thousand thoughts. I suggest 4:00am - 4:00am in my house. You? </p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\n\t\t\t\n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a \n</span>\n\t</p>\n\n\n</div>\n\n\n</article>\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\n    \n\n\n\n\n<!-- entry shared -->\n\n<article class="post entry">\n\n\n\n<!-- DISPLAY FULL POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/turns-out-its-a-summer-of-severe-illness-and-death.html">Turns Out It\'s a Summer of Severe Illness and Death</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a2eeca07e1200d-pi"><img alt="President Biden Winter of death" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202a2eeca07e1200d img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a2eeca07e1200d-450wi" style="width: 450px; display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="President Biden Winter of death" /></a>If you read entertainment and sports news sites, it seems that it&#39;s celebs and sports stars who are being overwhelmed, collapsing and some are dying &quot;suddenly.&quot;&#0160; &quot;Suddenly&quot; used to be a euphemism for suicide. &quot;After a long illness&quot; implied cancer. With less stigma than in the past, suicides and cancer deaths are more readily described in newspaper reports.&#0160; <a href="https://www.usmagazine.com/celebrity-news/pictures/celebrity-deaths-in-2022-stars-weve-lost/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">US Magazine just posted and article about celebrity deaths.</a><br /><br />Just yesterday, 32 year old Canadian comedian <a href="https://www.nbcnews.com/pop-culture/pop-culture-news/comedian-nick-nemeroff-dies-32-rcna35699" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Nick Nemeroff died</a> suddenly in his sleep. He had made a joke about Ivermectin on Christmas Eve, with a bandaid on his arm. <a href="https://pagesix.com/2022/06/27/danny-bonaduce-mystery-illness-affected-speech-walking/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Danny &quot;I will shake your foundation&quot; (Partridge) Bonaduce has&#0160; been stricken with a mystery illness</a> that has left him unable to speak or walk properly. Kourtney Kardashian&#39;s husband <a href="https://www.usmagazine.com/celebrity-news/news/travis-barker-reportedly-hospitalized-kourtney-by-his-side/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Travis Barker was rushed to Cedars Sinai</a> from a smaller LA hospital. Justin Bieber has a disfigured face due to Ramsay Hunt Syndrome (a rare side effect of the Covid vaccine), and his beautiful young wife Hailey had a stroke.<br /><br />Correlation does not equal causation. We&#39;re not making light of any of these deaths or illnesses. I&#39;d like to see life insurance actuarial reports for the last several years. Have there been more deaths among people under 60, have the statistics changed? Insurers bet that you will NOT die, while you pay your premiums. Payouts are a problem. <br /><br />Age of Autism focuses on autism, but we branch into many topics. Now that babies as young as 6 months can be vaccinated for Covid, it behooves us to keep an open mind and hopeful hearts that we won&#39;t see an increase in infant heart problems and worse.<br /><br />1967 was The Summer of Love.&#0160; And 2022?<br /><br /><br /><br /></p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\n\t\t\t\n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/special-education-crisis-in-the-british-isles.html">Special Education Crisis in the British Isles</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a30d4143f3200b-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="Abadnonned school" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202a30d4143f3200b img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a30d4143f3200b-250wi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="Abadnonned school" /></a>By Anne Dachel<br /><br />As anyone looking at <a href="https://www.lossofbraintrust.com/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">LossOfBrainTrust</a> can see, the majority of my stories are from Britain and Ireland currently. Things are in crisis all over the British Isles. Everywhere there\xe2\x80\x99s more funding for special education. Counties are building their own special schools, specifically ones for kids with autism.</p>\r\n<p>Official evaluations show schools are failing miserably when it comes to addressing the needs of those in special education. Story after story features special needs kids without a school place for this fall. Children wait years just for an evaluation to be classified as needing special help in school.</p>\r\n<p>The phrase \xe2\x80\x9cincreasing demand\xe2\x80\x9d is a regular feature in news coverage on special education in both Ireland and Britain.</p>\r\n<p>What do these stories tell us? Simple, there are more and more disabled children in these countries. It\xe2\x80\x99s not a secret. They keep telling us about it.</p>\r\n<p><strong>Bedfordshire: </strong></p>\r\n<p><em>\xe2\x80\x9cThat\xe2\x80\x99s more than 6,000 children in our mainstream schools on stage two of the SEND code of practice and around 3,000 with EHCPs\xe2\x80\xa6.</em></p>\r\n<p><em>CBC\xe2\x80\x99s director of children services Sarah-Jane Smedmor said: \xe2\x80\x9cWe\xe2\x80\x99ve seen that demand for EHCPs double in the last few years. So it\xe2\x80\x99s inevitable we need to ensure we meet the needs of our children individually.</em></p>\r\n<p><strong>Also from Bedfordshire: </strong></p>\r\n<p>Parents to protest lack of special ed services.</p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t    <p class="entry-more-link font-entrybody"><a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/special-education-crisis-in-the-british-isles.html#more">Continue reading "Special Education Crisis in the British Isles" &raquo;</a></p>\n                        \n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info fa-facebook"></i></a>\n     \n</span>\n\t</p>\n\n\n</div>\n\n\n</article>\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\n    \n\n    \n\n    \n\n    \n\n\n\n\n<!-- entry shared -->\n\n<article class="post entry">\n\n\n\n<!-- DISPLAY FULL POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/british-drug-regulator-mhra-develops-manufactures-and-sells-its-own-biological-products-including-va.html">British Drug Regulator (MHRA) Develops, Manufactures and Sells Its Own Biological Products Including Vaccines</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a30d410e84200b-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="John Stone UK Column" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202a30d410e84200b img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a30d410fa7200b-pi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="John Stone UK Column" /></a>By John Stone</p>\r\n<p><strong>(UPDATE)&#0160;It is disturbing to have confirmed by <a href="https://childrenshealthdefense.org/defender/who-gates-polio-vaccine-united-kingdom/#comment-5900677912">Megan Redshaw\xe2\x80\x99s article in The Defender</a>&#0160; yesterday &#0160;(June 27) that it will be the Gates/WHO/MHRA polio vaccine which is being rolled out in the UK which according to Dr Mark Bailey is not \xe2\x80\x9cproved\xe2\x80\x9d or in layman\xe2\x80\x99s language \xe2\x80\x9cexperimental\xe2\x80\x9d. Obviously, the Salk oral polio vaccine has not been in use for many years and his comparison is misleading and inappropriate , and we do not know why this product is preferred to the standard inactivated product (IPV).</strong></p>\r\n<p>This is a follow on to a UK Column Report last week with excellent analysis by retired nurse Debi Evans and News anchor Brian Gerrish which focused on the board meeting of the MHRA of Tuesday June 21. There were many disturbing features in the report which runs from 1.06.50 <a href="https://www.ukcolumn.org/video/uk-column-news-23rd-june-2022" rel="noopener" target="_blank">on the link</a>, but one really surprising fact which emerged - and I have been following the MHRA closely since at least 2004 - is that they combine purported role as a regulator of the biologics industry with developing its own biological products and trading with the industry: this happens through its subsidiary since 2013 the National Institute of Biological Standards and Control (NIBSC) though it\xe2\x80\x99s &#0160;not immediately clear how long NIBSC has traded its own biological products.</p>\r\n<p>Of particular relevance is that coincidentally with this meeting a new polio scare was being launched in the UK - no one as of this present time has been diagnosed with polio but polio has been detected <a href="https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/health-61896411" rel="noopener" target="_blank">in a North East London sewer</a>. It is therefore fascinating to follow the conversation (which I have transcribed as best I can) between to the interim director of NIBSC, Mark Bailey, and Stephen Lightfoot, Chairman of MHRA (<a href="https://www.ukcolumn.org/video/uk-column-news-23rd-june-2022" rel="noopener" target="_blank">at 1.22.18</a>):</p>\r\n<p>Bailey:</p>\r\n<p><em>Significant investment by NIBSC and also its partners the Gates foundation and of course its&#0160;part of&#0160; &#0160;the WHO lab in (indecipherable) and of course basically premiere eradication. There are three strains of polio and the team at NIBSC developed three different vaccines. It happens&#0160;that strain two is the one that has been deployed most in clinical trials in Africa and it&#39;s listed product by the WHO which mean it can be used in emergency situations even though it is not proved. We are now moving to clinical trials with the other two strains as well, so it&#39;s very exciting: it&#39;s a huge huge combination: its effect is that this vaccine cannot revert. So the Salk vaccine which was used with most of us as kids there was always a low chance of it reverting back to wild type which means things like polio begins to appear in the population. This is a great leap forward here because it can&#39;t revert so basically its much safer.<br /></em></p>\r\n<p>Lightfoot:</p>\r\n<p><em>Again I think this is a great example of how the MHRA is different from other regulators around the world because we have NIBSC or National Institute for Biological&#0160;Standards and Control where do some basic looking at fundamental research and this is a good example of the work that we are doing in that area and the public health benefit it can have internationally and not just in the UK&#0160; so I think actually as regulator we&#39;ve got some really important you know constituent parts that actually make us a very strong and&#0160;capable organisation.</em></p>\r\n<p>The reality of this is if the MHRA ever was functionally a \xe2\x80\x9cregulator\xe2\x80\x9d it has abandoned this role to facilitate business, it even trades with industry in <a href="https://www.nibsc.org/products/brm_product_catalogue/sub_category_listing.aspx?category=Vaccines&amp;subcategory=Coronavirus+(V)" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Coronavirus spike-protein</a>. This was emphasised in an earlier UK Column report when MHRA CEO June Raine excruciatingly discussed transforming the MHRA in 2020 from being \xe2\x80\x9ca regulator to an enabler\xe2\x80\x9d (<a href="https://www.ukcolumn.org/ukcolumn-news/uk-column-news-16th-june-2022" rel="noopener" target="_blank">at 47.30</a>). And of course it is a whole different level of concern if the MHRA not only received research funding <a href="https://www.gov.uk/government/news/mhra-awarded-over-980000-for-collaboration-with-the-bill-and-melinda-gates-foundation-and-the-world-health-organisation" rel="noopener" target="_blank">from the Gates Foundation</a> as has previously been identified but is actually in business with them (and the WHO). Of course, the pretext was that there was an emergency and this was in the most formal bureaucratic terms <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/the-british-government-the-world-health-organization-and-global-coup-of-2020.html" rel="noopener" target="_blank">an outright lie</a>.</p>\r\n\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t    <p class="entry-more-link font-entrybody"><a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/british-drug-regulator-mhra-develops-manufactures-and-sells-its-own-biological-products-including-va.html#more">Continue reading "British Drug Regulator (MHRA) Develops, Manufactures and Sells Its Own Biological Products Including Vaccines" &raquo;</a></p>\n                        \n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" href="https://profile.typepad.com/rescuepost">Age of Autism</a> on June 27, 2022 at 12:01 AM in <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/current_affairs/">Current Affairs</a>, <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/john-stone-uk/">John Stone</a>, <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/science/">Science</a>, <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/vaccines/">Vaccine Safety</a> </span> <span class="separator">|</span> <a class="permalink" href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/british-drug-regulator-mhra-develops-manufactures-and-sells-its-own-biological-products-including-va.html">Permalink</a>\n\n \n\t<span class="separator"> | entry">\n\n\n\n<!-- DISPLAY FULL POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/pickles-pretzels-and-pop-tarts.html">Pickles, Pretzels and Pop Tarts</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a308d37bd8200c-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="Snack graphic" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202a308d37bd8200c img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a308d37bd8200c-250wi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="Snack graphic" /></a>By Cathy Jameson</p>\r\n<p>An FB memory from 2010 had me smiling last week:&#0160; <em>I </em><em>love Ronan more than the last bread and butter pickle left in the house. &#0160;Usually he gobbles them up. &#0160;Happily, he turned it down so I could eat it. &#0160;I could eat those tasty treats all day long.</em></p>\r\n<p>Ironically, that memory popped up the day after I again had the last bread and butter pickle.&#0160; I didn\xe2\x80\x99t offer that last one to Ronan though.&#0160; I didn\xe2\x80\x99t want to share it.&#0160; I wanted it all for myself.&#0160; I don\xe2\x80\x99t usually do that; but that one night when I wanted just a little peace and quiet, I ate that last pickle.&#0160;</p>\r\n<p>And I enjoyed it.&#0160;</p>\r\n<p>The next day, after reading that memory, I could\xe2\x80\x99ve felt stabs of regret for not sharing.&#0160; But I didn\xe2\x80\x99t.&#0160; That\xe2\x80\x99s because I had a brand new bottle of pickles ready for Ronan.&#0160; Seeing the new jar in the pantry reminded me of a shopping trip he and I took many years ago.&#0160; Outings these days aren\xe2\x80\x99t always successful for him, but that day all those years ago, with tons of patience and great communication, it was one of his best days\xe2\x80\xa6</p>\r\n<p><em>From another memory, written and shared with family, back in the spring of 2015\xe2\x80\xa6Enjoy!</em></p>\r\n<p>Ronan continues to be on a modified school schedule.&#0160; Lacking energy to sustain a full academic day, he only attends a few hours of school each week.&#0160; Since starting the modified schedule, I\xe2\x80\x99ve had to do a lot of juggling. &#0160;Finding someone to watch Ronan during the day doesn\xe2\x80\x99t always work out, so he ends up accompanying me wherever I need to go.&#0160;</p>\r\n<p>Errands are harder.&#0160;</p>\r\n<p>Getting to appointments takes longer.</p>\r\n<p>Meetings take careful planning. &#0160;</p>\r\n<p>Since we\xe2\x80\x99re always hoping Ronan will gain more independence, I welcome the opportunity to bring him with me. &#0160;Most of the time, it works out well having Ronan tagalong to places he normally wouldn&#39;t go. &#0160;He gets to see his community during regular business hours.&#0160; He gets to learn and master new skills.&#0160; He gets to interact with people and they with him. &#0160;</p>\r\n<p>As much as I\xe2\x80\x99d rather he could have the energy to be at school learning, he\xe2\x80\x99s been able to learn valuable lessons when we go out. &#0160;Some simple things he\xe2\x80\x99s had to learn over the last year include:</p>\r\n<p>-Learning how to walk calmly to the car when prompted (instead of acting out because he wanted to stay home and watch more YouTube videos).</p>\r\n<p>-Staying buckled in the car seat (instead of attempting to wiggle out because we didn\xe2\x80\x99t get more French fries).</p>\r\n<p>-Keeping shoes (and clothes) on while we shop (instead of taking them off when things didn\xe2\x80\x99t go as planned).</p>\r\n<p>-Keeping shoes on while we\xe2\x80\x99re in the car (instead of throwing them at Mommy while she\xe2\x80\x99s driving).</p>\r\n<p>-Resisting a meltdown and remaining calm (<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2014/06/a-typical-birthday-turned-terribly-wrong.html" rel="noopener" target="_blank">instead of thrashing about on the floor</a> as has happened before).&#0160;</p>\r\n<p>-Using appropriate communication (instead of pulling Mommy\xe2\x80\x99s hair when we went down the \xe2\x80\x9cwrong\xe2\x80\x9d grocery store aisle).</p>\r\n<p>Being able to learn those simple things has helped when we go out and about, but Ronan still has lots yet to learn.&#0160; I do as well.&#0160; I need to plan my time better so that I\xe2\x80\x99m not rushing Ronan into situations he\xe2\x80\x99s not comfortable.&#0160; I need to prepare the environment better as well as prepare those who will interact with Ronan.&#0160; For instance, when Ronan must accompany me to a doctor\xe2\x80\x99s appointment that I\xe2\x80\x99ve scheduled for myself, I should remember to show Ronan a picture of where we\xe2\x80\x99re going or at least drive by the place with him one time before we actually need to go in it.&#0160; I should also let the provider know that my visit may take a few minutes longer than usual.&#0160; That\xe2\x80\x99s because Ronan\xe2\x80\x99s curiosity, as well as his anxiety and his sensory issues, can prevent a smooth transition into (or out of) the parking lot\xe2\x80\xa6the waiting room\xe2\x80\xa6the exam room\xe2\x80\xa6or meeting room that we\xe2\x80\x99re going into. &#0160;I need to remember that sometimes things will take longer. &#0160;That things won&#39;t go as planned. That we are that try, try, try, try one more time family. &#0160;I also need to remember one more thing. </p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t    <p class="entry-more-link font-entrybody"><a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/pickles-pretzels-and-pop-tarts.html#more">Continue reading "Pickles, Pretzels and Pop Tarts" &raquo;</a></p>\n                        \n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" href="https://profile.typepad.com/rescuepost">Age of Autism</a> on June 26, 2022 at 06:00 AM in <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/cathy-jameson/">Cathy Jameson</a> </span> <span class="separator">|</span> <a class="permalink" href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/pickles-pretzels-and-pop-tarts.html">Permalink</a>\n\n \n\t<span class="separator"> | </span>\n\t\n\t\t\t <a class="entry-comments" \n</span>\n\t</p>\n\n\n</div>\n\n\n</article>\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\n    \n\n\n\n\n<!-- entry shared -->\n\n<article class="post entry">\n\n\n\n<!-- DISPLAY FULL POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/required-viewing-like-its-1974.html">Required Viewing - Like It\'s 1974</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a30d40c14a200b-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="Free_to_Be..._You_and_Me_(album_cover)" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202a30d40c14a200b img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a30d40c14a200b-250wi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="Free_to_Be..._You_and_Me_(album_cover)" /></a>A year ago, Americans lost their jobs and their right to attend restaurants, concerts, sporting events and other activities if they did NOT choose the Covid vaccine.&#0160; Americans did not have the right to say no, which is a choice. Yesterday, we had another version of change in choice with the SCOTUS decision on Roe v. Wade. The right to say yes was affected. The divisions between Americans are growing by the minute. Up is down. Left is right. Right is middle. Middle is long gone. Imagine my surprise when my daughter started listening to a single song on YouTube, a song I hadn&#39;t heard in many years. Free To Be You and Me. The song debuted with a book and full album in 1974 as a way to bring Americans TOGETHER in understanding and acceptance. Back in those days, the topics were &quot;simpler.&quot; Black, white, boys and girls. End racism. End sexism. Seems quaint by today&#39;s complicated standards. But I think that Free To Be You And Me has more value then ever. As a look back, it shows we could and did make progress. As a look today, it shows we still need more. One group near and dear to our hearts, has been left behind in the society of free choice - those who chose not and/or are unable to vaccinate per the CDC guidelines. If medical choice matters, it has to matter from all sides, does it not?&#0160; If you&#39;ve never watched Free to Be You And Me - or listened to the lyrics of each star-studded song, I encourage you to take trip back to 1974. <br /><br /></p>\r\n<p><em>Free to Be... You and Me is a children&#39;s entertainment project, conceived, created and executive-produced by actress and author Marlo Thomas. Produced in collaboration with the Ms. Foundation for Women,[1] it was a record album and illustrated book first released in November 1972 featuring songs and stories sung or told by celebrities of the day (credited as &quot;Marlo Thomas and Friends&quot;) including Alan Alda, Rosey Grier, Cicely Tyson, Carol Channing, Michael Jackson, Roberta Flack, Shirley Jones, Jack Cassidy, and Diana Ross. An ABC television special, also created by Thomas, using poetry, songs, and sketches, followed two years later in March 1974. The basic concept was to encourage post-1960s gender neutrality, saluting values such as individuality, tolerance, and comfort with one&#39;s identity. A major thematic message is that anyone\xe2\x80\x94whether a boy or a girl\xe2\x80\x94can achieve anything.</em></p>\r\n<p><br /><br /><iframe allow="accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture" allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="315" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/7PS3nOcLbHI" title="YouTube video player" width="460"></iframe></p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\n\t\t\t\n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" href="https://profile.typepad.com/rescuepost">Age of Autism</a> on June 25, 2022 at 06:00 AM in <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/parents_corner/">Dreams</a> </span> <span class="separator">|</span> <a class="permalink" href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/required-viewing-like-its-1974.html">Permalink</a>\n\n \n\t<span class="separator"> | </span>\n\t\n\t\t\t <a class="entry-comments" href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/required-viewing-like-its-1974.html#comments">Comments (10)</a>\n\t\n\n\n          </p>\n\n\n          <!-- technorati tags -->\n\n\n\n \n</span>\n\t</p>\n\n\n</div>\n\n\n</article>\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n<!-- entry shared -->\n\n<article class="post entry">\n\n\n\n<!-- DISPLAY FULL POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/action-alert-let-people-with-disabilities-on-ssi-have-10000-in-assets-.html">Action Alert: Let People with Disabilities on SSI Have $10,000 in Assets </a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a2eec94107200d-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="Action alert" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202a2eec94107200d img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a2eec94107200d-115wi" style="width: 102px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="Action alert" /></a>Note: Below is an action alert from the ARC, and it&#39;s super important for those of us whose children are adults on SSI - Supplemental Security Income.&#0160; Since 1989, the asset limit has been $2000. There&#39;s a bill to increase that to $10,000 so that individuals like my own daughters can have some money set aside for emergencies. No one can live on SSI - certainly not in 2022. And everyone needs an emergency fund. Parents have been supplementing SSI forever. My daughters couldn&#39;t live here in Connecticut and pay rent, utilities, food, clothing, etc. even with their COMBINED SSI.&#0160; They live with me, their unpaid Group Home Manager and 3 shift support staff.&#0160; Uncle Sam is USING parents to foot the bill. And telling them they CAN NOT save a dime over $2000 for their future needs. <br /><br /><a href="https://action.thearc.org/VynIJ0a?p2asource=email-062422" rel="noopener" target="_blank">CLICK HERE TO SEND THE ALERT</a><br /><br />###<br /><br /><strong>Tell Congress: Support the SSI Savings Penalty Elimination Act NOW!</strong></p>\r\n<p>The Supplemental Security Income (SSI) program provides critical support for millions of people with disabilities to be able to afford necessities like food and rent. But it has many rules that make it hard for people to save money and get out of poverty. SSI has an asset limit that has not been updated since 1989. Assets include money in bank accounts, retirement accounts, and savings. Right now, people who get SSI can only have $2,000 in assets. Married couples can only have $3,000.</p>\r\n<p>These asset limits mean that people cannot save money and force people with disabilities into poverty.</p>\r\n<p><a href="https://action.thearc.org/VynIJ0a?p2asource=email-062422" rel="noopener" target="_blank">TAKE ACTION</a>: Urge your U.S Senators to support people with disabilities and their families by cosponsoring the bipartisan SSI Savings Penalty Elimination Act (S.4102) which would raise these asset limits.</p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\n\t\t\t\n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" href="https://profile.typepad.com/rescuepost">Age of Autism</a> on June 24, 2022 at 06:00 AM </span> <span class="separator">|</span> <a class="permalink" href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/action-alert-let-people-with-disabilities-on-ssi-have-10000-in-assets-.html">Permalink</a>\n\n fab fa-facebook"></i></a>\n     \n</span>\n\t</p>\n\n\n</div>\n\n\n</article>\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\n    \n\n\n\n\n<!-- entry shared -->\n\n<article class="post entry">\n\n\n\n<!-- DISPLAY FULL POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/autism-woke-the-pie-in-the-sky-failure-of-the-autism-speaks-autism-treatment-network.html">Autism Woke: The Pie in the Sky Failure of The Autism Speaks Autism Treatment Network</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a30d407d5c200b-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="Fish needs a bicycle" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202a30d407d5c200b img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a30d407d5c200b-250wi" style="width: 227px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="Fish needs a bicycle" /></a>You couldn&#39;t design a worse system than anything launched by Autism Speaks. The Autism Treatment Network is, as&#0160; my dear old Dad used to say, &quot;Like the sleeves off their vest.&quot; Or my favorite, &quot;Like a fish needs a bicycle.&quot; Useless.&#0160; Katie Wright details the travesty - well funded, back pats galore, fully employed professionals, University cred, all while individuals suffer and families slip deeper into debt, despair and doubt.<br /><br />###<br /><br /></p>\r\n<p>&#0160;The Autism Speaks Treatment Network is an embarrassment.</p>\r\n<p>In twelve years of its existence, ATN received tens of millions of taxpayer dollars and accomplished virtually nothing. ATN gives new meaning to setting a low bar in autism research.We know how low the bar is, so that&#39;s quite an accomplishment!&#0160; Autism Speaks and the NIH should cease funding wasteful project immediately.</p>\r\n<p>ATN was founded because autism families were having an impossible time finding medical care for their children. This is especially true regarding ASD kids with GI problems. In the waiting room of Christian\xe2\x80\x99s pediatric GI, I regularly meet parents from PA, OH, MD and other far away states. It should not be so difficult to find a GI who knows how to treat our kids.</p>\r\n<p>The NIH has yet to fund 1 ASD/GI clinical treatment study. ATN was created to fill that gap. They were supposed to do urgently needed medical treatment research. Treatment research, not just addressing GI problems, but autoimmune conditions, PANDAS, intractable seizures, etc\xe2\x80\xa6..</p>\r\n<p>However none of that happened. The director of ATN for twelve years, is, incredibly, a speech therapist! That says everything you need to know about ATN\xe2\x80\x99s commitment to helping medically affected autistic kids. The vast majority of ATN research is redundant, dated or useless, telling us what we already know.</p>\r\n<p>For 12 yrs ATN has researched ASD sleep problems behaviorally only!! This is inhumane. A friend took her son to their Vanderbilt sleep clinic and, of course, none of ATN\xe2\x80\x99s \xe2\x80\x9ctreatments,\xe2\x80\x9d basically sleep hygiene, worked.</p>\r\n<p>When behavioral interventions don\xe2\x80\x99t work for night wakefulness you must immediately look into biological causation of sleeplessness. In my son\xe2\x80\x99s cause it was an overgrowth of candida causing the sleep problems. The rashes are a giveaway. Elimination of sugar, simple carbs and a round of antifungals stopped this seemingly intractable problem. This problem was destroying my family. We had not sleep through the night for years. Other families should no longer be suffering this fate.</p>\r\n<p>ATN\xe2\x80\x99s GI research is basically give the kid Miralax! Ok, we did that in 2000! Since then we have learned that Miralax is incredibly toxic and should not be given to anyone under the age of 17! CHOP did a study exposing the fact that Miralax contains an excessive amount of arsenic!</p>\r\n<p>These are just some of the ridiculous ATN research you have financed:</p>\r\n<p>1)&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; Causes of obesity in ASD kids. Guess what?? Bad food and lack of exercise!!</p>\r\n<p>2)&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; Relationship between GI problems and stress! Yes! They are related!</p>\r\n<p>3)&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; Association of repetitive behavior and sleeplessness. Helping no one and telling us what we already know.</p>\r\n<p>4)&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; Communication deficits often associated with motor system deficits. Once again, research helping no one leading to nothing.</p>\r\n<p>5)&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; Creatine deficiency in ASD kids. This was established almost 20 yrs ago.</p>\r\n<p>6)&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; Parents of ASD kids suffer from chronic stress!! And grass is green!</p>\r\n<p>7)&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; Caregiver education level and ASD child with sleep issues. I find this just plain insulting,</p>\r\n<p>8)&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; Decreased Sound tolerance in ASD kids. NO!! Shocking</p>\r\n<p>9)&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; Medical care and associations with depression. Who isn\xe2\x80\x99t depressed when they need medical help?</p>\r\n<p>11)&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; Walking! Walking is a possible option for promoting exercise in obese ASD people. I mean, can you even believe this??</p>\r\n<p>12)&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; Sex differences in repetitive behavior. Families have really been clamoring for this one!</p>\r\n<p>13) &#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; Behavior impairments can be caused by sleep problems. Yes, they ARE related!</p>\r\n<p>14)&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; Hand-writing problems in autism. A top priority in autism community!</p>\r\n<p>I\xe2\x80\x99ll tell you what ATN did not study- treatment for GI disease, treatment for PANDAS, treatment for immune deficiencies (IVIG), intractable seizures and CBD, food allergies (a large % of ASD kids have undx celiac or gluten intolerance conditions).</p>\r\n\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t    <p class="entry-more-link font-entrybody"><a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/autism-woke-the-pie-in-the-sky-failure-of-the-autism-speaks-autism-treatment-network.html#more">Continue reading "Autism Woke: The Pie in the Sky Failure of The Autism Speaks Autism Treatment Network" &raquo;</a></p>\n                        \n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span target="_blank"><i class="icon fab fa-facebook"></i></a>\n     \n</span>\n\t</p>\n\n\n</div>\n\n\n</article>\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\n    \n\n\n\n\n<!-- entry shared -->\n\n<article class="post entry">\n\n\n\n<!-- DISPLAY FULL POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/vaccination-and-chronic-disease.html">53 Years of Knowledge: Vaccination and Chronic Disease</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a2eec8ff46200d-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="Truthfyl gentle fearless" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202a2eec8ff46200d img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a2eec8ff46200d-250wi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="Truthfyl gentle fearless" /></a>Imagine if doctors around the world acknowledged and fought to end vaccine injury. Wouldn&#39;t that be something? Instead, they actively work to deny and gaslight patients and their families.&#0160; Start paying attention to obituaries and articles about young people, including children, dying of natural causes and &quot;peacefully.&quot; Dr. Moskowitz is truthful, gentle (I&#39;ve had the privilege of meeting him) and fearless.<br /><br />###</p>\r\n<p>You can find a .pdf of this post here. <span class="asset  asset-generic at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202a2eec8ff26200d img-responsive"><a href="https://www.rescuepost.com/files/dr-richard-moskowitz-vaccination-and-chronic-disease.pdf">Download Dr Richard Moskowitz Vaccination and Chronic Disease</a></span>&#0160; Dr. Moskowitz meticulously formatted and cited his article, however, the blog platform is not always kind to formatting. I encourage you to read the .pdf.&#0160; Thank you. <br /><br />By Richard Moskowitz, M. D.</p>\r\n<p>In my 53 years as a family doctor, I cared for a large number of children who were adversely affected by many different vaccinations, with diagnoses as varied as an average pediatric practice. &#0160;Yet they all reacted in closely similar fashion, hinting at something important in the nature of chronic disease, the great riddle that has confounded physicians since the earliest times. &#0160;My plan is to begin with a summary of my own clinical experience, together with pertinent findings in the scientific literature, and then explore the questions it raises about chronicity itself, a dysfunction that somehow manages to insinuate itself into our everyday physiology, achieves in effect a new &quot;normal&quot; of healthy and diseased modes co-existing side-by-side in place of the old, and resists cure by perpetuating itself over the lifetime.&#0160; With all that in mind, I&#39;ll finish with the COVID to bring everything up date, followed by a brief epilogue on the special vantage point of clinical practice.</p>\r\n<p><strong>1.</strong></p>\r\n<p><strong>Chronic disease is everywhere.</strong></p>\r\n<p>Always a troubling enigma to physicians, chronic diseases have become so prevalent in in recent decades that they now command a preponderance of the time, space, and energy of most practicing physicians in the United States and the developed world<strong>.</strong>&#0160; As far back as 2008, the CDC surveyed the incidence of six prominent types in the United States -- diabetes, cardiovascular disease, COPD, asthma, cancer, and arthritis -- and found that</p>\r\n<p>60% of all adults had been diagnosed with 1 or more of them, as had</p>\r\n<p>78% of those 55 and older, and</p>\r\n<p>85.6% of those 65 and older,</p>\r\n<p>and that</p>\r\n<p>40% of all adults had been diagnosed with 2 or more, as had</p>\r\n<p>47% of those 55 and older, and</p>\r\n<p>56% of those 65 and older.<sup>1</sup></p>\r\n<p>Since then, the fractions of our population affected by the most common ones have been estimated as follows, taking them one by one:<br /><br />asthma, COPD, and chronic lung disease - 15% of all adults<sup>2,3</sup>&#0160; &#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;<br />arthritis - 23% of all adults<sup>4<br /></sup>hypertension - 33% of all adults, 76% of ages 75-84<sup>5</sup> &#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;<br />obesity - 42% of all adults<sup>6</sup> &#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; <br />diabetes - 10% of all adults<sup>7</sup> &#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; <br />chronic kidney disease - 15% of all adults<sup>8</sup>&#0160; &#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; &#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; <br />dementia - 14% by age 71<sup>9</sup>&#0160; &#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; <br />some form of cancer - 50% of males and 33% of females at some point in their lifetime<sup>10</sup>&#0160;&#0160;</p>\r\n<p>Although these figures have been steadily increasing throughout the industrialized world, the United States leads all other countries by a considerable margin, with by far the lowest life expectancy, despite spending the most per capita on health care.<sup>11</sup></p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t    <p class="entry-more-link font-entrybody"><a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/vaccination-and-chronic-disease.html#more">Continue reading "53 Years of Knowledge: Vaccination and Chronic Disease" &raquo;</a></p>\n                        \n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" href="https://profile.typepad.com/rescuepost">Age of Autism</a> on June 22, 2022 at 06:00 AM in <a \n</span>\n\t</p>\n\n\n</div>\n\n\n</article>\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\n    \n\n\n\n\n<!-- entry shared -->\n\n<article class="post entry">\n\n\n\n<!-- DISPLAY FULL POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/the-cruel-summer-of-2022.html">The Cruel Summer of 2022</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a308d2b551200c-pi"><img alt="Diving board" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202a308d2b551200c img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a308d2b551200c-250wi" style="width: 250px; display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="Diving board" /></a><br />Happy first day of summer. As early as today, parents will feel the pressure from their pediatricians to give the Covid vaccine(s) to their babies as young as 6 months old. Popsicles.&#0160; Sandcastles. Swim lessons and high dive test jumps. But is there any water in the pool?&#0160;&#0160;</p>\r\n<p><iframe allow="accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture" allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="315" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/l9ml3nyww80" title="YouTube video player" width="460"></iframe><br />###</p>\r\n<p><a href="https://www.cnn.com/2022/06/18/health/children-under-5-covid-vaccine-explainer-wellness/index.html" rel="noopener" target="_blank">The FDA has authorized Covid-19 vaccines for children under 5. What should parents know?</a></p>\r\n<p>The US Food and Drug Administration gave emergency use authorization on Friday for both the Pfizer/BioNTech and Moderna vaccines for young children. Vaccine advisers to the US Centers for Disease Control and Prevention voted unanimously on Saturday in support of giving babies and other kids as young as 6 months a Covid-19 vaccination.<br /><br />CDC Director Dr. Rochelle Walensky signed off on the plan, clearing the way for the vaccinations to be administered as early as next week.<br /><br />Parents may be reluctant to actually get them when they become available, an April survey found. Just 18% of parents of children under 5 said they would vaccinate their child against Covid-19 as soon as a vaccine became available, according to an April Kaiser Family Foundation Vaccine Monitor survey.</p>\r\n<p>Nearly 40% of those surveyed said they would &quot;wait and see&quot; before vaccinating their young children, 11% said they would get the vaccine for their kids only if required, and 27% said they would &quot;definitely not&quot; get the Covid-19 vaccination for their child.</p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\n\t\t\t\n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" href="https://profile.typepad.com/rescuepost">Age of Autism</a> on June 21, 2022 at 06:00 AM in <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/vaccines/">Vaccine Safety</a> </span> <span class="separator">|</span> <a class="permalink" href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/the-cruel-summer-of-2022.html">Permalink</a>\n\n \n\t<span class="separator"> | </span>\n\t\n\t\t\t <a class="entry-comments" \n</span>\n\t</p>\n\n\n</div>\n\n\n</article>\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\n    \n\n\n\n\n<!-- entry shared -->\n\n<article class="post entry">\n\n\n\n<!-- DISPLAY FULL POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/the-explosion-in-special-education-is-autism.html">The Explosion in Special Education is Autism</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<div class="photo-wrap photo-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202a2eec88eb9200d" id="photo-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202a2eec88eb9200d" style="float: left; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px; width: 250px;"><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a2eec88eb9200d-pi"><img alt="Autism check" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202a2eec88eb9200d img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a2eec88eb9200d-250wi" style="width: 250px;" title="Autism check" /></a>\r\n<div class="photo-caption caption-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202a2eec88eb9200d" id="caption-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202a2eec88eb9200d">Parents &amp; Schools Pay the Bill</div>\r\n</div>\r\n<p>Note: We&#39;re seeing the result of normalizing autism over the last 25 years. From a diagnosis to a difference.&#0160; From awareness and action to acceptance and acquiescence. Autism has been scooted over to something in the sexual category.&#0160; The &quot;approved&quot; symbol is a rainbow infinity loop.&#0160; The rainbow has one meaning today and it&#39;s not Oz. The red, blue, yellow puzzle piece is considered discriminatory. Schools are overwhelmed with special education students, and severely behavioral students. It&#39;s not that teachers can&#39;t teach all of a sudden. The raw material, the kids, are not of the same neurological status, meaning quality. Tomorrow, it will start to get much worse. It&#39;s Covid vaccine day starting at 6 months. I hope we&#39;re still here in 6 years when that cohort starts school, the ones who live.<br /><br />###<br /><br />By Anne Dachel<br /><br />IT\xe2\x80\x99S REALLY ALL ABOUT AUTISM.</p>\r\n<p>Seriously.</p>\r\n<p>Autism, that perpetual mystery identified by the iconic multicolored puzzle piece is a condition rampant in kids today. We\xe2\x80\x99ve learned to accept and even celebrate the disorder.</p>\r\n<p><strong>Reality</strong></p>\r\n<p>With literally THOUSANDS of stories on the decline of children everywhere on my site, LossOfBrainTrust.com, <a href="https://www.lossofbraintrust.com/">https://www.lossofbraintrust.com/</a> it\xe2\x80\x99s an undisputable fact that autism or some other form of neurological damage has changed traditional childhood.</p>\r\n<p>(We call this damage by a lot of different names: autism, Aspergers, ADD, ADHD, OCD, speech, language and communication needs (SLCN), social/emotional disorder (SED), severe learning difficulties (SLD), and many more acronyms.)</p>\r\n<p>And it\xe2\x80\x99s getting worse right before our eyes. Something is happening to children\xe2\x80\x99s brains that make them unable to speak in many cases, unable to learn normally and unable to behave as children have always been expected to behave.</p>\r\n<p>We congratulate ourselves for recognizing the sorrowful condition of children and continually call for better detection and earlier intervention, as if those improvements would solve all the problems of dysfunctional children worldwide.</p>\r\n<p>I\xe2\x80\x99m in my sixth year posting stories on LossOfBrainTrust, yet clearly this is a disaster that goes unrecognized, even by the people involved. Officials keep funding more special ed classrooms and even whole schools, but it\xe2\x80\x99s never enough. We\xe2\x80\x99re constantly told that THERE ARE MORE DISABLED CHILDREN without even an attempt at an explanation for why it\xe2\x80\x99s happening.</p>\r\n<p>And kids are increasingly MORE SEVERELY DISABLED. That fact is sometimes noted in news reports, again in passing, but it should scare everyone.</p>\r\n<p>A story I found recently is a good example of what\xe2\x80\x99s happening to children.</p>\r\n<p><strong>Wiscasset, ME:</strong> <strong>Wiscasset\xe2\x80\x99s special education needs rise</strong></p>\r\n\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t    <p class="entry-more-link font-entrybody"><a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/the-explosion-in-special-education-is-autism.html#more">Continue reading "The Explosion in Special Education is Autism" &raquo;</a></p>\n                        \n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" href="https://profile.typepad.com/rescuepost">Age of Autism</a> on June 20, 2022 at 06:00 AM in <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/media/">Anne Dachel</a> </span> <span class="separator">|</span> <a class="permalink" href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/the-explosion-in-special-education-is-autism.html">Permalink</a>\n\n \n\t<span class="separator"> | </span>\n\t\n\t\t\t <a tags -->\n\n\n\n          <!-- post footer links -->\n\t<p class="entry-footer-share entry-footer-share-buttons">\n\t\t<span class="entry-footer-links-twitter">\n     <a target="_blank"><i class="icon fab fa-twitter"></i></a>\n</span> <span class="separator">|</span> <span class="entry-footer-links-plusone"></span> <span class="separator">|</span> <span \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/canwetalkaboutit.html">#CanWeTalkAboutIt</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a308d2784d200c-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="Time to talk" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202a308d2784d200c img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a308d2784d200c-250wi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="Time to talk" /></a>By Cathy Jameson</p>\r\n<p>Can we talk about it?&#0160;</p>\r\n<p>YES, talk about it.&#0160;</p>\r\n<p>I wish more people would.&#0160;</p>\r\n<p>What is \xe2\x80\x9cit\xe2\x80\x9d?&#0160;</p>\r\n<p>It\xe2\x80\x99s the thing that must not be named, you know\xe2\x80\xa6<em>*</em>whispers* <em>the covid vaccine..</em>.&#0160;</p>\r\n<p>Many have already shared tons about \xe2\x80\x9cit\xe2\x80\x9d and about other \xe2\x80\x9cits\xe2\x80\x9d over the years.&#0160; When I think back to when I first wanted to know more about vaccines, I think of the OG, the original voices who spoke up.&#0160; Those voices spoke for a growing many.&#0160; Their vaccine stories were heard in <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=09H6Gp-Y9XQ" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Washington, D.C. back in 1999</a>.&#0160; Parent-founded groups had <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2009/02/generation-rescue-ad-in-usa-today-court-again-concedes-vaccines-cause-autism.html" rel="noopener" target="_blank">lots to say back in the day</a> about it and were able to get their message in print, too.&#0160; Others <a href="https://www.imdb.com/title/tt3715598/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">shared their plight</a> and other important information <a href="https://1986theact.com/watch/"></a> in more <a href="https://1986theact.com/watch/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">recent documentaries</a>. &#0160;</p>\r\n<p>Fast forward to now, and a new generation of people want to talk about it.&#0160; They want what it\xe2\x80\x99s done to them and their livelihoods to be known for all to see.&#0160;</p>\r\n<p>They join thousands of others who\xe2\x80\x99ve questioned vaccines after vaccine injury.&#0160; Those others have \xe2\x80\x98taken it to the streets\xe2\x80\x99 before and <a href="https://abcnews.go.com/GMA/OnCall/story?id=4987758" rel="noopener" target="_blank">marched in our nation\xe2\x80\x99s capital</a>. &#0160; They\xe2\x80\x99ve caught the <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2008/06/post-1.html" rel="noopener" target="_blank">ear of influential people</a> who\xe2\x80\x99ve also offered to help the cause.&#0160; Over the years, moms headed to their own state capitals to rally the people. &#0160;From <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2015/04/laura-hayes-speech-on-parental-rights-and-medical-freedom-california-sb277-.html" rel="noopener" target="_blank">one side of the country</a> to <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2015/04/maine-national-town-hall-debate-on-vaccines.html" rel="noopener" target="_blank">the other</a>, moms got their message about it out there.&#0160; <a href="https://newjersey.news12.com/former-professional-fighter-says-vaccines-are-to-blame-for-sons-death-38999281" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Dads</a> did, <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=KXwUoI_0AWw" rel="noopener" target="_blank">too. </a></p>\r\n<p>It isn\xe2\x80\x99t just parents and patients who\xe2\x80\x99ve raised their voices and their concerns; some medical people were on the right side of truth and kept the conversation going as well.&#0160; They knew it was worth <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2015/06/dr-toni-bark-on-ca-sb277.html" rel="noopener" target="_blank">talking about vaccines</a>.&#0160; But not enough people in the mainstream medical community want to warn that these liability-free medical products are risky.</p>\r\n<p>Instead, it remains the patient themselves, or their parents, to keep raising their voices about vaccines and vaccine injuries.&#0160;</p>\r\n<p>The further we get back into real life with fewer restrictions, the less I hear some people talking about the covid vaccine.&#0160; Of course, certain others (mainstream news talking heads, corporate media, and Hollywood spokespeople) still can\xe2\x80\x99t say enough about it.&#0160; They insist that it\xe2\x80\x99s the only defense we have against the covid illness.&#0160; They believe it\xe2\x80\x99s the safest thing for you.&#0160;</p>\r\n<p>People\xe2\x80\x99s personal stories say otherwise.</p>\r\n<p>So, can we talk about it, the covid vax?&#0160; Sure!&#0160; Yes!&#0160; Why not!&#0160; They are still under Emergency Use Authorized (EUA).&#0160; They are still causing a divide among families.&#0160; They all still come with potential risk, <a href="https://magneticmediatv.com/2022/06/novavax-approved-by-fda-in-covid-19-fight/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">even the new one</a> that the FDA <a href="https://magneticmediatv.com/2022/06/novavax-approved-by-fda-in-covid-19-fight/"></a> recently recommend for EUA. &#0160;</p>\r\n<p>Of course, we should talk about them, these covid vaccines.&#0160; We should because the propaganda has not waned.&#0160; The risks have not lessened.&#0160; And the side effects, ones known and ones yet to be discovered, are very real.</p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t    <p class="entry-more-link font-entrybody"><a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/canwetalkaboutit.html#more">Continue reading "#CanWeTalkAboutIt" &raquo;</a></p>\n                        \n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" href="https://profile.typepad.com/rescuepost">Age of Autism</a> on June 19, 2022 at 06:00 AM in <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/cathy-jameson/">Cathy Jameson</a> </span> <span class="separator">|</span> <a class="permalink" href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/canwetalkaboutit.html">Permalink</a>\n\n \n\t<span class="separator"> | </span>\n\t\n\t\t\t <a class="entry-comments" href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/canwetalkaboutit.html#comments">Comments (5)</a>\n\t\n\n\n          </p>\n\n\n          <!-- technorati tags -->\n\n\n\n          <!-- post footer links -->\n\t<p class="entry-footer-share entry-footer-share-buttons">\n\t\t<span class="entry-footer-links-twitter">\n     <a class="icon fab fa-pinterest"></i></a>\n\n</span> <span class="separator">|</span> <span class="entry-footer-links-facebook_like">\n     \n     <a href="https://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.ageofautism.com%2F2022%2F06%2Fcanwetalkaboutit.html" target="_blank"><i class="icon fab fa-facebook"></i></a>\n     \n</span>\n\t</p>\n\n\n</div>\n\n\n</article>\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\n    \n\n\n\n\n<!-- entry shared -->\n\n<article class="post entry">\n\n\n\n<!-- DISPLAY FULL POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/cardiology-theres-a-great-future-in-pediatric-cardiology-will-you-think-about-it.html">Cardiology. There\'s a Great Future in Pediatric Cardiology. Will You Think About It?</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a308d25d5c200c-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="Risk" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202a308d25d5c200c img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a308d25d5c200c-250wi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="Risk" /></a>The Covid vaccine will be added to the current recommendation at 6 months for a grand total of 8 diseases covered in one visit at 6 months of age with 1 or 2 follow up visits for the second &amp; third doses. That&#39;s 9 or 10 vaccines in a matter of weeks. How many readers remember being told that the first seizure your child had was benign, a mere febrile seizure? Common. Nothing to worry about. Resolves itself. And then you faced intractable seizures. That&#39;s what the CDC is saying about the myocarditis and pericarditis following the Covid vaccines. <em>&quot;...most cases of myocarditis associated with the Moderna and Pfizer-BioNTech COVID-19 vaccines are characterized by rapid resolution of symptoms following conservative management, with no impact on quality of life reported by most patients who were contacted for follow-up at 90 days or more after reporting myocarditis.&quot; </em>There&#39;s an old line from The Graduate, &quot;Plastics. There&#39;s great future in plastics. Will you think about it?&quot; It&#39;s graduation season right now. &quot;Pediatric cardiology. There&#39;s a great future in pediatric cardiology. Will you think about it?</p>\r\n<p><em>At 6 months of age, your baby should receive vaccines to protect them from the following diseases:</em></p>\r\n<p><em>Diphtheria, tetanus, and whooping cough (pertussis) (DTaP) (3rd dose)</em><br /><em>Haemophilus influenzae type b disease (Hib) (3rd dose)</em><br /><em>Polio (IPV) (3rd dose)</em><br /><em>Pneumococcal disease (PCV13) (3rd dose)</em><br /><em>Rotavirus (RV) (3rd dose)</em></p>\r\n<p>From The CDC, a press release on the approval of Moderna and Pfizer Covid vaccines for babies 6 months and older. <br /><strong><br />Coronavirus (COVID-19) Update: FDA Authorizes Moderna and Pfizer-BioNTech COVID-19 Vaccines for Children Down to 6 Months of Age</strong></p>\r\n<p>Today, the U.S. Food and Drug Administration authorized emergency use of the Moderna COVID-19 Vaccine and the Pfizer-BioNTech COVID-19 Vaccine for the prevention of COVID-19 to include use in children down to 6 months of age.</p>\r\n<p>For the Moderna COVID-19 Vaccine, the FDA amended the emergency use authorization (EUA) to include use of the vaccine in individuals 6 months through 17 years of age. The vaccine had been authorized for use in adults 18 years of age and older.<br />For the Pfizer-BioNTech COVID-19 Vaccine, the FDA amended the EUA to include use of the vaccine in individuals 6 months through 4 years of age. The vaccine had been authorized for use in individuals 5 years of age and older.</p>\r\n<p>Key points:</p>\r\n<p>The FDA\xe2\x80\x99s evaluation and analysis of the safety, effectiveness and manufacturing data of these vaccines was rigorous and comprehensive, supporting the EUAs. The agency determined that the <span style="color: #ff0000;">known and potential benefits</span> of the Moderna and Pfizer-BioNTech COVID-19 vaccines outweigh the <span style="color: #ff0000;">known and potential risks</span> in the pediatric populations authorized for use for each vaccine.<br /><br />Prior to making the decision to authorize these vaccines for the respective pediatric populations, the FDA\xe2\x80\x99s independent Vaccines and Related Biological Products Advisory Committee was consulted and voted in support of the authorizations.</p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t    <p class="entry-more-link font-entrybody"><a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/cardiology-theres-a-great-future-in-pediatric-cardiology-will-you-think-about-it.html#more">Continue reading "Cardiology. There\'s a Great Future in Pediatric Cardiology. Will You Think About It?" &raquo;</a></p>\n                        \n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" href="https://profile.typepad.com/rescuepost">Age of Autism</a> on June 18, 2022 at 06:00 AM in <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/vaccines/">Vaccine Safety</a> </span> <span class="separator">|</span> <a class="permalink" href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/cardiology-theres-a-great-future-in-pediatric-cardiology-will-you-think-about-it.html">Permalink</a>\n\n \n\t<span class="separator"> | </span>\n\t\n\t\t\t <a class="entry-comments" href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/cardiology-theres-a-great-future-in-pediatric-cardiology-will-you-think-about-it.html#comments">Comments (9)</a>\n\t\n\n\n   <a href="https://twitter.com/share?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.ageofautism.com%2F2022%2F06%2Fcardiology-theres-a-great-future-in-pediatric-cardiology-will-you-think-about-it.html&text=Cardiology.%20The..." target="_blank"><i class="icon fab fa-twitter"></i></a>\n</span> <span class="separator">|</span> <span class="entry-footer-links-plusone"></span> <span class="separator">|</span> <span Vote Saturday on Moderna and Pfizer for Infants and Toddlers</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" Substack:<br /><br /><a href="https://tobyrogers.substack.com/p/breaking-news-cdc-launches-sneak" rel="noopener" target="_blank">BREAKING NEWS: CDC launches sneak attack; the ACIP will meet TOMORROW (Friday, June 17) and Saturday, June 18 to extend the mRNA Final Solution to little kids</a><br /><br />The White House has kept these meetings a secret until now <br /><br />`I\xe2\x80\x99m the first to report this breaking national news:</p>\r\n<p>This morning I listened to the meeting of the National Vaccine Advisory Committee. Melinda Wharton gave her update from CDC... and they have scheduled a special two day meeting of the Advisory Committee on Immunization Practices (ACIP) for TOMORROW (Friday, June 17) and Saturday (June 18). The agenda is here:</p>\r\n<p><a href="https://www.cdc.gov/vaccines/acip/meetings/downloads/agenda-archive/agenda-2022-06-17-18-508.pdf" rel="noopener" target="_blank">https://www.cdc.gov/vaccines/acip/meetings/downloads/agenda-archive/agenda-2022-06-17-18-508.pdf</a></p>\r\n<p>Friday they will discuss safety, immunogenicity, and efficacy of Moderna in kids 6 months through 5 years of age AND Pfizer in kids 6 months through 4 years of age. Saturday they will vote. The entire process is set up to rubber stamp the VRBPAC meetings from yesterday.</p>\r\n<p>When White House \xe2\x80\x9cCovid-19 Czar\xe2\x80\x9d Ashish Jha went on TV earlier in the week and said that these shots would be available by June 19, he surely knew that these meetings were in the works. But they kept them secret from the public until Melinda Wharton let the cat out of the bag this morning.</p>\r\n<p>Apparently, the CDC is going to hold off on debating Moderna in kids 6 to 17 years old until next week (they have another meeting scheduled for June 22 and 23). <strong>The CDC has decided to target the littlest kids first. </strong></p>\r\n<p><strong>What is to be done.</strong></p>\r\n<p>Let\xe2\x80\x99s light \xe2\x80\x98em up right now.   </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a30d3f666e200b-pi" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a30d3f666e200b-250wi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="Vaccine piper" /></a><em>A forced march: A movement of military prisoners faster or in more adverse conditions than would be normal to tire them excessively.</em><br /><br />###</p>\r\n<p><a href="https://abcnews.go.com/Health/fda-committee-clears-kids-17-vaccine-option-moderna/story?id=85388359" rel="noopener" target="_blank">From ABC News</a>: A committee of advisers at the Food and Drug Administration voted unanimously Tuesday in favor of authorizing the Moderna vaccine for kids ages 6 through 17, paving the way to add one more vaccine to the options available for this age group.</p>\r\n<p>Currently, <a href="https://abcnews.go.com/Health/fda-accepts-pfizer-application-covid-vaccine-kids-clearing/story?id=85114427" rel="noopener" target="_blank">only Pfizer\xe2\x80\x99s vaccine</a> is available for kids over 5 years old. Moderna\xe2\x80\x99s vaccine, which was stalled in the regulatory process for months, would give parents another option.</p>\r\n<p>The process to get Moderna\xe2\x80\x99s vaccine out to pharmacies and clinics now moves to FDA leadership, which must decide whether to issue an official emergency use authorization of the vaccine.<a href="https://abcnews.go.com/Health/us-lift-covid-testing-requirement-air-travelers-enter/story?id=85308831"></a></p>\r\n<p>After that, the Centers for Disease Control and Prevention\xe2\x80\x99s team of advisers will review Moderna\xe2\x80\x99s data, and finally, CDC Director Rochelle Walensky will issue her recommendation.</p>\r\n<p>It&#39;s not clear whether adding Moderna as another option in the vaccine arsenal will <a href="https://abcnews.go.com/Health/doctors-advise-kids-11-boosted-covid-vaccination-rates/story?id=85133917" rel="noopener" target="_blank">move the needle for uptake in the kids</a> and adolescent age group. <a href="https://abcnews.go.com/Health/fda-committee-clears-kids-17-vaccine-option-moderna/story?id=85388359" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Read more (and weep.)</a></p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\n\t\t\t\n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/gut-science-was-slower-than-a-colon-after-surgery.html">Gut Science Was Slower Than A Colon After Surgery</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a308d1d678200c-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="Microbiome7" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202a308d1d678200c img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a308d1d678200c-250wi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="Microbiome7" /></a>Dr. Andy Wakefield thrust the gut connection into the spotlight more than 20 years ago. &quot;Science&quot; is slower than a colon after surgery. And often treats the originators like.....&#0160; From <a href="https://safeminds.org/news/antibiotics-exposure-in-pregnancy-affects-the-gut-microbiota-in-offspring/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Safeminds</a>:<br /><br />June 13, 2022</p>\r\n<p><a href="https://safeminds.org/news/antibiotics-exposure-in-pregnancy-affects-the-gut-microbiota-in-offspring/" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><strong>Gut Bacteria Alterations Are Dependent on Offspring\xe2\x80\x99s Sex</strong></a></p>\r\n<p>To prevent <a href="https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC3938141/">newborn sepsis caused by maternal Group B <em>Streptococcus</em></a> exposure, antibiotic use was promoted during labor and delivery starting in the 1990s. Since then, the use of prophylactic antibiotics given to laboring mothers has increased to more than <a href="https://academic.oup.com/ije/article/33/1/2/668235?login=true">30% of all deliveries in the United States</a>. However, this practice was implemented before our present-day and still emerging understanding of the microbiota\xe2\x80\x99s important role in many aspects of health. Recently, researchers at the MIND Institute published a study investigating the effect of antibiotics administered to pregnant mice on offspring gut microbiome composition and metabolic capabilities. The researchers also investigated how these microbiota changes can influence the offspring\xe2\x80\x99s immune responses. The study\xe2\x80\x99s design involved administering a broad-spectrum antibiotic orally to pregnant mice during late gestation through birth. Post-birth, bacterial DNA was taken from offspring fecal samples and was then sequenced and analyzed. The offspring\xe2\x80\x99s serum and brain tissue cytokine levels were also analyzed. The results showed that the antibiotic cocktail given to the pregnant mice produced significant diversity and taxonomic changes in their offspring\xe2\x80\x99s microbiome. Also altered in the offspring were genomic and metabolic pathways. Interestingly, an increased <em>Firmicutes/Bacteroidetes </em>(F/B) ratio was found in female offspring but not males. An increased F/B ratio is associated with dysbiosis and metabolic disorders. The MIND Institute researchers concluded that maternal antibiotic exposure could produce long-lasting effects on the offspring\xe2\x80\x99s gut microbiome and neuroimmune responses. They believe their findings demonstrate how important the role of the early microbiome is in the development of gastrointestinal and immune systems.&#0160;</p>\r\n<p><a href="https://www.mdpi.com/2227-9059/10/5/1042/htm" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Original Study</a></p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\n\t\t\t\n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n class="icon fab fa-pinterest"></i></a>\n\n</span> <span class="separator">|</span> <span class="entry-footer-links-facebook_like">\n     \n     <a href="https://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.ageofautism.com%2F2022%2F06%2Fgut-science-was-slower-than-a-colon-after-surgery.html" target="_blank"><i class="icon fab fa-facebook"></i></a>\n     \n</span>\n\t</p>\n\n\n</div>\n\n\n</article>\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\n    \n\n    \n\n\n\n\n<!-- entry shared -->\n\n<article class="post entry">\n\n\n\n<!-- DISPLAY FULL POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/many-infant-deaths-classified-as-sids-are-actually-caused-by-vaccines.html">Many Infant Deaths Classified as SIDS Are Actually Caused by Vaccines</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a30d3f1494200b-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="Baby coffin" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202a30d3f1494200b img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a30d3f1494200b-250wi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="Baby coffin" /></a>Crib death. Cot death. SIDS has been a formal cause of death since 1969.&#0160; It&#39;s hard to imagine a deeper pain. Today, we have <a href="https://www.nzherald.co.nz/lifestyle/what-is-sads-healthy-young-people-dying-from-sudden-adult-death-syndrome/TIOAK4SYPF5LFSKP5QZCVG23IM/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">SADS</a> - and you can guess what the A stands for - adult. Healthy young people, not infants, dying of &quot;natural&quot; causes. As always, thank you to Dr. Gaunt for speaking out on behalf of pediatric health and wellness. <br /><br />By Dr. William H. Gaunt, NMD</p>\r\n<p><strong>What Is SIDS?</strong></p>\r\n<p>Sudden Infant Death Syndrome (SIDS) is defined as: \xe2\x80\x9cThe sudden death of an infant under one year of age which remains unexplained after a thorough case investigation, including performance of a complete autopsy, examination of the death scene, and review of the clinical history.\xe2\x80\x9d It is the leading cause of death in children between one month and one year of age. As we see in the definition, the cause of SIDS is unexplained or unknown. This classification is a convenient place to hide infant deaths caused by vaccines.</p>\r\n<p><strong>Before and After 1979</strong></p>\r\n<p>There are 130 official ways for an infant to die. These are listed in the International Classification of Diseases and are sanctioned by WHO and CDC. Before 1979, one of the possible causes of infant death was vaccines. After 1979, all cause-of-death classifications associated with vaccination were eliminated. (Thanks to Neil Z. Miller for this and other information used in this article. He published \xe2\x80\x9cVaccines and sudden infant death: An analysis of the VAERS database 1990-2019 and review of the medical literature\xe2\x80\x9d in PubMed Central Toxicology Reports on June 24th, 2021). Before 1979, a coroner could choose vaccines as the cause of an infant death if the evidence fit that conclusion. After 1979, vaccines were no longer one of the accepted causes of infant death and the coroner would be forced to choose another cause of death. SIDS would be a likely alternative choice. It is not a stretch to assume that the vaccine companies had a hand in eliminating vaccines as one of the accepted possible causes of infant deaths.</p>\r\n<p><strong>Infant Deaths Occur Far More Frequently Within 7 Days After Receiving Multiple Vaccines</strong></p>\r\n<p>The CDC vaccine schedule calls for the hepatitis B vaccine to be given on the day of birth. At 2 months, it calls for 8 vaccines (diphtheria, tetanus, pertussis (DTaP), polio, hepatitis B, pneumococcal, haemophilus B, and rotovirus.) At 4 months, it calls for 7 vaccines (DTaP, polio, pneumoccal, haemophilus B, and rotovirus.) Then at 6 months there are 9 more vaccines on the schedule (DTaP, polio, hepatitis B, pneumococcal, haemophilus B, flu, and rotovirus). No worries that 7 to 9 vaccines given to an infant at one time might kill some infants. The authorities routinely exonerate the vaccines and encourage the selection of SIDS as the appropriate cause of these deaths. VAERS (Vaccine Adverse Events Reporting System) data shows that more than 78% of reported infant deaths occurred within the first 7 days post-vaccination. This does not prove that vaccines killed these infants, but it is highly suspicious.</p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t    <p class="entry-more-link font-entrybody"><a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/many-infant-deaths-classified-as-sids-are-actually-caused-by-vaccines.html#more">Continue reading "Many Infant Deaths Classified as SIDS Are Actually Caused by Vaccines" &raquo;</a></p>\n                        \n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" href="https://profile.typepad.com/rescuepost">Age of Autism</a> on June 14, 2022 at 06:00 AM in <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/current_affairs/">Current Affairs</a>, <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/vaccines/">Vaccine Safety</a> </span> <span class="separator">|</span> <a class="permalink" href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/many-infant-deaths-classified-as-sids-are-actually-caused-by-vaccines.html">Permalink</a>\n\n \n\t<span class="separator"> | </span>\n\t\n\t\t\t <a class="entry-comments" href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/many-infant-deaths-classified-as-sids-are-actually-caused-by-vaccines.html#comments">Comments (11)</a>\n\t\n\n\n          </p>\n\n\n          <!-- technorati tags -->\n\n\n\n          <!-- post footer links -->\n\t<p class="entry-footer-share entry-footer-share-buttons">\n\t\t<span class="entry-footer-links-twitter">\n     <a class="entry-footer-links-pinterest">\n     <a
