class="icon fab fa-pinterest"></i></a>\n\n</span> <span class="separator">|</span> <span class="entry-footer-links-facebook_like">\n     \n     <a href="https://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.ageofautism.com%2F2022%2F06%2Fmany-infant-deaths-classified-as-sids-are-actually-caused-by-vaccines.html" target="_blank"><i class="icon fab fa-facebook"></i></a>\n     \n</span>\n\t</p>\n\n\n</div>\n\n\n</article>\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\n    \n\n    \n\n    \n\n    \n\n\n\n\n<!-- entry shared -->\n\n<article class="post entry">\n\n\n\n<!-- DISPLAY FULL POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/the-british-government-the-world-health-organization-and-global-coup-of-2020.html">The British Government, the World Health Organization and the Global Coup of 2020</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a308d178a3200c-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="UK lockdown" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202a308d178a3200c img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a308d178a3200c-250wi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="UK lockdown" /></a>By John Stone</p>\r\n<p><strong><em>In March 2020 the British Government decided to impose lockdown on the determination of the WHO against the advice of its own medical experts including Sir Chris Whitty - the experts then followed the policy, subordinating their judgment to the outside agency. These events anticipated the WHO\xe2\x80\x99s recent and continuing attempts to formalise global supremacy in health, and demonstrates the arbitrariness and chaos which will inevitably follow&#0160;</em></strong></p>\r\n<p>I am trying to understand the events of March 2020 in the light of an answer to a recent Freedom of Information Request. Why and how was it that four days before lockdown was imposed on March 23 the four Chief Medical Officers of the United Kingdom posted a notice on-line announcing that COVID-19 had been downgraded <u>from</u> the status of High Consequence Infectious Disease (HCID).</p>\r\n<p>This peculiar event has not gone entirely un-noticed but has never really been explained. Before this point the disease named in the document &#0160;as COVID-19 (rather than &#0160;identified as virus SARS-CoV-2) - was a \xe2\x80\x9chigh consequence infectious disease\xe2\x80\x9d, while almost at the very instant our lives, and everyone\xe2\x80\x99s, &#0160;were to be irrevocably pitched into turmoil with the denial of civil liberties and most basic human rights, untold economic destruction and chaos, it was no longer so designated.</p>\r\n<p>If the disease was no longer \xe2\x80\x9chigh consequence\xe2\x80\x9d there could be absolutely no reason for this high level and prolonged disruption, and yet it was at this precise moment that the inevitability of lockdown started to be promoted, only to be confirmed four days later. But according to the CMOs\xe2\x80\x99 reckoning at no point in the past two and a quarter years, whatever actions they took to restrict our lives or coerce us to accept injections of novel products, has the disease been \xe2\x80\x9chigh consequence\xe2\x80\x9d.&#0160;</p>\r\n<p>This anomaly cannot I believe be stressed enough: my FOI request produced no new documents but the Department of Health and Social Care drew my attention to <a href="https://questions-statements.parliament.uk/written-questions/detail/2020-09-28/95975" rel="noopener" target="_blank">a Parliamentary answer by Jo Churchill on November 6, &#0160;2020</a>&#0160;to Conservative MP John Redwood (submitted fully 5 and a half weeks before on September 28):</p>\r\n<p><em>The four nations public health high consequence infectious disease (HCID) group made an interim recommendation in January 2020 to classify COVID-19 as an HCID, based on the information that was available during the very early stages of the outbreak.</em></p>\r\n<p><em>Once more was known about COVID-19, United Kingdom public health bodies reviewed the available information against the HCID criteria and noted certain changes. These changes included the increase in information available about mortality rates, which are low overall amongst the general population; greater clinical awareness; and the availability of a specific and sensitive laboratory test for the virus.</em></p>\r\n<p><em>COVID-19 has not been considered a HCID in the UK since 19 March 2020, but this reclassification has not affected the Government\xe2\x80\x99s response to COVID-19, which remains a comprehensive national effort.</em></p>\r\n<p>So, the junior minister, Jo Churchill, confirmed that decision was made with due consideration and not because of some expedience: this remained the case on November 6, 2020, and remains the case today because whatever the CMOs have said subsequently to the public, notably government Chief Medical Officer Sir Chris Whitty they have not updated this statement.</p>\r\n<p>With this in mind let us go back and look at what was said <a href="https://www.gov.uk/guidance/high-consequence-infectious-diseases-hcid" rel="noopener" target="_blank">in the statement of March 19, 2020</a>&#0160;:it may be one of those occasions when British government documents are more revealing than most.</p>\r\n<p><em>As of 19 March 2020, COVID-19 is no longer considered to be a high consequence infectious disease (HCID) in the UK. There are many diseases which can cause serious illness which are not classified as HCIDs.</em></p>\r\n<p><em>The 4 nations public health HCID group made an interim recommendation in January 2020 to classify COVID-19 as an HCID. This was based on consideration of the UK HCID criteria about the virus and the disease with information available during the early stages of the outbreak. Now that more is known about COVID-19, the public health bodies in the UK have reviewed the most up to date information about COVID-19 against the UK HCID criteria. They have determined that several features have now changed; in particular, more information is available about mortality rates (low overall), and there is now greater clinical awareness and a specific and sensitive laboratory test, the availability of which continues to increase.</em></p>\r\n<p><em>The Advisory Committee on Dangerous Pathogens (ACDP) is also of the opinion that COVID-19 should no longer be classified as an HCID.</em></p>\r\n\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t    <p class="entry-more-link font-entrybody"><a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/the-british-government-the-world-health-organization-and-global-coup-of-2020.html#more">Continue reading "The British Government, the World Health Organization and the Global Coup of 2020" &raquo;</a></p>\n                        \n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/type-it-out.html">Type It Out</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a2eec7549a200d-pi"><img alt="Listen and learn typewriter" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202a2eec7549a200d img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a2eec7549e200d-pi" style="width: 297px; display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="Listen and learn typewriter" /></a><br />Note: Grab a coffee, this post has donuts! No, really. Keep reading.<br /><br />By Cathy Jameson</p>\r\n<p>Ronan can sign his basic wants and needs.&#0160; He can type them out also.&#0160; We continue to pray that he will one day regain speech, but until that happens we encourage Ronan to communicate in ways he\xe2\x80\x99s able to.&#0160;</p>\r\n<p>One night last week, when he couldn\xe2\x80\x99t sleep, he came to my room and sat on the edge of my bed.&#0160; He\xe2\x80\x99s a quiet kind of guy, unless his favorite songs or movies are playing.&#0160; Then, Ronan can be really REALLY loud \xe2\x80\x93 to the point the kids will politely move him and his ipad to another room.&#0160; They don\xe2\x80\x99t want to squash his happiness; they just don\xe2\x80\x99t want to hear all of that happiness right next to them. &#0160;When Ronan came and sat on my bed, he was exceptionally quiet.&#0160; I knew he wanted something but couldn\xe2\x80\x99t figure out what.&#0160; My laptop was open, so I quickly asked Ronan to type to me.&#0160; The prompt I gave him was, Hey, Ronan, what do you want?</p>\r\n<p><em>mom my lijke ipad</em></p>\r\n<p>ronan, it&#39;s bedtime</p>\r\n<p><em>mom my like ipad&#0160;</em></p>\r\n<p>it&#39;s too late to play. it&#39;s time for bed.&#0160;</p>\r\n<p><em>mom my like ipad&#0160;</em></p>\r\n<p>you can play on the ipad in the morning. it&#39;s very late, so it&#39;s bedtime now.&#0160;</p>\r\n<p><em>mom my like ipad</em></p>\r\n<p>no, thank you.</p>\r\n<p><em>mom my like ipad</em></p>\r\n\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t    <p class="entry-more-link font-entrybody"><a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/type-it-out.html#more">Continue reading "Type It Out" &raquo;</a></p>\n                        \n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n \n</span>\n\t</p>\n\n\n</div>\n\n\n</article>\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\n    \n\n    \n\n\n\n\n<!-- entry shared -->\n\n<article class="post entry">\n\n\n\n<!-- DISPLAY FULL POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/action-alert-tell-the-fda-to-get-their-hands-off-our-children.html">Action Alert: Tell the FDA to Get Their Hands Off Our Children</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a308d12a60200c-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="AlignAct_VRBAC_Still_6.7a" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202a308d12a60200c img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a308d12a60200c-250wi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="AlignAct_VRBAC_Still_6.7a" /></a>Almost 15 years ago, Age of Autism posted its first article about vaccines and the autism epidemic. Today, thousands of posts and hundreds of thousands of comments and a million tears later, we&#39;re still helping sound the alarm that vaccination choice is a civil, medical and moral right. Once the Covid vaccines are approved for babies and toddlers, they are likely to end up on the pediatric schedule with protection from liability and little chance for the average parent to decline. Imagine yearly boosters, and playing Russian Roulette with myocarditis. If it&#39;s required for day care, school, camps, well, parents will comply to make childhood a little smoother. Smoother. We know better. We&#39;ve learned the hard way. Children&#39;s Health Defense has a tightly organized call to action asking all of us to tell the FDA - NO.&#0160; Below is an excerpt and link.&#0160; Please click over to see how you can spread the word to your loved ones, friends, colleagues and and&#0160; social media followers who might unfriend and unfollow you. Next week is critical.<br /><strong><br />###<br /><br />Watch Mary Holland explain in <a href="https://rumble.com/v17kapr-tell-the-fda-no-authorization-of-covid-shots-for-babies-and-children.html" rel="noopener" target="_blank">a brief video</a>.<br /></strong></p>\r\n<p><a href="https://childrenshealthdefense.org/child-health-topics/take-action/action-alert-tell-the-fda-to-get-their-handsoffourchildren/" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><strong>Action Alert: Tell the FDA to Get Their #HandsOffOurChildren</strong></a></p>\r\n<p>The U.S. Food and Drug Administration (FDA) is declaring war on our children and it\xe2\x80\x99s on each of us to be unrelenting as we defend the next generation from Big Pharma and its allies. We must stop the FDA\xe2\x80\x99s attack, beginning with a campaign to end unethical and unsubstantiated Emergency Use Authorizations (EUA) that will subject our younger and most vulnerable children to the unnecessary risks of COVID shots.</p>\r\n<p><strong><a href="https://alignact.com/go/tell-the-fda-to-get-their-handsoffourchildren">Take Action: Tell the FDA No EUA of COVID Shots for Babies and Children</a></strong></p>\r\n<p>The FDA\xe2\x80\x99s Vaccines and Related Biological Products Advisory Committee (VRBPAC) is <a href="https://www.fda.gov/news-events/fda-meetings-conferences-and-workshops" rel="noopener" target="_blank">scheduled to meet</a> on four separate occasions in June to discuss additional EUAs that would provide cradle-to-grave COVID shots and consider a \xe2\x80\x9c<a href="https://childrenshealthdefense.org/defender/fda-pfizer-moderna-skip-trials-covid-vaccines/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Future Framework</a>\xe2\x80\x9d that will permanently lower the bar for safety and efficacy going forward.</p>\r\n<p>Their itinerary is as follows:</p>\r\n<ul>\r\n<li><a href="https://www.fda.gov/advisory-committees/advisory-committee-calendar/vaccines-and-related-biological-products-advisory-committee-june-7-2022-meeting-announcement" rel="noopener" target="_blank">June 7</a> \xe2\x80\x94 Emergency Use Authorization for Novavax\xe2\x80\x99s COVID shot for adults.</li>\r\n<li><a href="https://www.fda.gov/advisory-committees/advisory-committee-calendar/vaccines-and-related-biological-products-advisory-committee-june-14-15-2022-meeting-announcement" rel="noopener" target="_blank">June 14</a> \xe2\x80\x94 Amendment to Moderna\xe2\x80\x99s EUA to include primary series to children and adolescents 6 through 17 years of age.</li>\r\n<li><a href="https://www.fda.gov/advisory-committees/advisory-committee-calendar/vaccines-and-related-biological-products-advisory-committee-june-14-15-2022-meeting-announcement" rel="noopener" target="_blank">June 15</a> \xe2\x80\x94 Amendment to Moderna\xe2\x80\x99s EUA to include primary series for children 6 months to 5 years and amendment to Pfizer\xe2\x80\x99s EUA to include the primary series to children 6 months through 4 years of age.</li>\r\n<li><a href="https://www.fda.gov/advisory-committees/advisory-committee-calendar/vaccines-and-related-biological-products-advisory-committee-june-28-2022-meeting-announcement#event-information" rel="noopener" target="_blank">June 28</a> \xe2\x80\x94 Proposed \xe2\x80\x9cFuture Framework\xe2\x80\x9d for COVID shots.</li>\r\n</ul>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\n\t\t\t\n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" href="https://profile.typepad.com/rescuepost">Age of Autism</a> on \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/dr-andy-wakefield-and-childrens-health-defense-films-announce-the-premiere-of-infertility-a-diabolic.html">Dr. Andy Wakefield and Children\xe2\x80\x99s Health Defense Films Announce the Premiere of \xe2\x80\x98Infertility: A Diabolical Agenda\xe2\x80\x99</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><em> <a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a308d1047a200c-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="InfertilityPoster_6.2f-691x1024" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202a308d1047a200c img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a308d1047a200c-250wi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="InfertilityPoster_6.2f-691x1024" /></a>New documentary exposes a WHO program resulting in the sterilization of African women without their knowledge or consent.</em></p>\r\n<p><strong>Austin, TX</strong> \xe2\x80\x93 From award-winning filmmaker Dr. Andy Wakefield, in collaboration with executive producer Robert F. Kennedy, Jr. and Children\xe2\x80\x99s Health Defense (CHD) Films comes the documentary \xe2\x80\x9c<a href="https://infertilitymovie.org/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Infertility: A Diabolical Agenda.</a>\xe2\x80\x9d The film exposes a World Health Organization (WHO) <a href="https://www.scirp.org/journal/paperinformation.aspx?paperid=81838" rel="noopener" target="_blank">population control experiment</a> carried out under the guise of a vaccination program, resulting in the sterilization of women in Africa without their knowledge or consent.</p>\r\n<p>The film will premiere on Friday, June 10 at 2:00 pm ET on <a href="https://live.childrenshealthdefense.org/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">CHD.TV</a>. Immediately following the 30-minute film, a special edition of CHD.TV\xe2\x80\x99s \xe2\x80\x9c<a href="https://live.childrenshealthdefense.org/shows/chd-friday-roundtable" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Friday Roundtable</a>\xe2\x80\x9d will feature special guests Dr. Andy Wakefield, Dr. Christiane Northrup, Dr. Jim Thorp, Dr. Brian Hooker and Dr. Liz Mumper to discuss the dramatic rise in infertility issues across the globe.</p>\r\n<p>\xe2\x80\x9cIt is with timely irony that the World Health Organization reveals its true colors as it makes a desperate grab for control of global health,\xe2\x80\x9d said director Dr. Andy Wakefield. \xe2\x80\x9cThis story is a true \xe2\x80\x98WHO\xe2\x80\x99 dunnit.\xe2\x80\x9d</p>\r\n<p>\xe2\x80\x9c<a href="https://infertilitymovie.org/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Infertility</a>\xe2\x80\x9d pulls back the curtain to reveal the truth behind WHO\xe2\x80\x99s nefarious collaboration with the Kenyan government in which an experimental tetanus vaccination, later found to be laced with the pregnancy hormone \xce\xb2hCG, was given to millions of unknowing African women of childbearing age. Consequently, their right to carry children was stolen. Wakefield chronicles this tragic story and brings shocking new evidence to light. As Dr. Stephen Karanja warns in the film, \xe2\x80\x9cWhen they\xe2\x80\x99re through with Africa, they\xe2\x80\x99re coming for you.\xe2\x80\x9d</p>\r\n<p>\xe2\x80\x9cThe truths exposed in this film cast a long shadow from a tetanus trial in Africa to the symptoms of infertility that are happening all over the world, including reports after the <a href="https://childrenshealthdefense.org/defender/gardasil-vaccine-linked-birth-rate-declines/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Gardasil vaccine</a> and the <a href="https://infertilitymovie.org/wp-content/uploads/COVID-19-and-the-surge-in-Decidual-Cast-Shedding.pdf" rel="noopener" target="_blank">COVID shots</a>,\xe2\x80\x9d said CHD chief science director Dr. Brian Hooker.</p>\r\n<p>\xe2\x80\x9cThis film documents evidence that strongly supports the idea that the WHO was conducting an experiment on women of childbearing age to make them infertile without informed consent,\xe2\x80\x9d said Mary Holland, CHD president, general counsel and author of <a href="https://www.amazon.com/HPV-Vaccine-Trial-Generation-Betrayed/dp/1510710809" rel="noopener" target="_blank">The HPV Vaccine On Trial: Seeking Justice For A Generation Betrayed</a>.</p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t    <p class="entry-more-link font-entrybody"><a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/dr-andy-wakefield-and-childrens-health-defense-films-announce-the-premiere-of-infertility-a-diabolic.html#more">Continue reading "Dr. Andy Wakefield and Children\xe2\x80\x99s Health Defense Films Announce the Premiere of \xe2\x80\x98Infertility: A Diabolical Agenda\xe2\x80\x99" &raquo;</a></p>\n                        \n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" href="https://profile.typepad.com/rescuepost">Age of Autism</a> on entry">\n\n\n\n<!-- DISPLAY FULL POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/part-3-frau-komas-second-coming-mass-murder-autism-and-the-cult-of-weaponized-genetics-.html">Part 3 Frau Koma\xe2\x80\x99s Second Coming:  Mass Murder, Autism and the Cult of Weaponized Genetics </a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e2017c35eca4e5970b-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="Frau K By Adriana Gamondes" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e2017c35eca4e5970b img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e2017c35eca4e5970b-400wi" style="width: 400px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="Frau K By Adriana Gamondes" /></a>Good morning, today we wrap up our revisit with Adriana Gamondes&#39; 3 part series on school shooters, pharma and in this installment, autism. <br /><br /><strong>Part 3, The Enlightened Rapture, Read <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2013/01/frau-komas-second-coming-mass-murder-autism-and-the-cult-of-weaponized-genetics.html" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Part 1</a> and <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2013/01/mass-murder-autism-and-the-cult-of-weaponized-genetics.html" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Part 2</a>.</strong></p>\r\n<p><em>Those who promise us paradise on earth never produced anything but a hell.</em> ~Karl Raimund Popper<strong>&#0160;</strong></p>\r\n<p>By Adriana Gamondes</p>\r\n<p>Autism, the fastest growing developmental disorder in the US, represents more than 7% of a $40 billion dollar<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2012/03/the-phoenicians-autism-recovery-denial-drug-profits-and-the-medias-flat-earth-2012.html" rel="noopener" target="_blank"> psychopharmaceutical market </a>for a demographic of roughly 1 to 2% of individuals under age 25, where roughly 85% of autism diagnoses are found. Marking a condition as a public safety hazard and those with the traits as near devils is the time honored manner of manufacturing public consent for exploitative and coercive treatment and dehumanization. In other words, a wide belief that those with autism are likely to kill could effectively snuff protest against drugging mandates which Torry, Satel, Koplewicz, NAMI, the American Psychiatric Association, the National Institute of Mental Health, a steady procession of presidential administrations and the pharmaceutical industry have pushed for all along.</p>\r\n<p>But the population with autism may be only one of many targets of this particular campaign. Autism research provides an endless supply of <a href="http://archpsyc.jamanetwork.com/article.aspx?articleid=1107328" rel="noopener" target="_blank">unsubstantiated genetic corollaries</a> which have the distinction of being protected by the state in order to obfuscate the role of government public health agencies in contributing to an epidemic. And, of course, these unsubstantiated genetic corollaries have endless applications for political and industrial exploits.</p>\r\n<p>Questioning the \xe2\x80\x9clargely genetic\xe2\x80\x9d foundations of autism has ruined medical, scientific and media careers, and this may partly be because, as with the elusive schizophrenia \xe2\x80\x9cgenes,\xe2\x80\x9d so many reputations and articles of scientific faith hinge on the theory. For instance, if a group of researchers needs to prove that pigs fly to serve an industrial sponsor or as part of an exercise in &quot;weaponized anthropology\xe2\x80\x9d targeting a strategic or ideological foe, all they need do is link \xe2\x80\x9cproofs\xe2\x80\x9d of the imaginary flight of pigs to autism to create an automatic credibility shield</p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t    <p class="entry-more-link font-entrybody"><a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/part-3-frau-komas-second-coming-mass-murder-autism-and-the-cult-of-weaponized-genetics-.html#more">Continue reading "Part 3 Frau Koma\xe2\x80\x99s Second Coming:  Mass Murder, Autism and the Cult of Weaponized Genetics " &raquo;</a></p>\n                        \n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" href="https://profile.typepad.com/rescuepost">Age of Autism</a> on June 09, 2022 at 06:00 AM </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a2eec6a4a5200d-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="Twitter Report" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202a2eec6a4a5200d img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202a2eec6a4a5200d-300wi" style="width: 300px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="Twitter Report" /></a>Disability or difference?&#0160; Let&#39;s get down to brass tacks. In the Age of Autism community, autism is a disability. It&#39;s not just a difference in my three daughters. They live under plenary guardianship. They rely on me for 100% of their health and safety and day to day life. They rely on the government for their $834 monthly Social insecurity, which I, like every parent here, supplement so that they have a roof over their heads. <br /><br />When I read the <a href="https://twitter.com/ageofautism" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Tweet</a> in the photo on Monday, I&#39;d about had it&#0160; ACCEPTANCE as a vanilla flag waving moment.&#0160; April came and went, a quiet month and&#0160; it was changed from AWARENESS to ACCEPTANCE.&#0160; We still believe in ACTION, never acquiescence. I reported the account for hate speech.&#0160; Below are some of the comments we had <a href="https://www.facebook.com/AgeofAutism/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">on our Facebook page</a> in response to the photo. We also need to be SEEN, HEARD and have PRIDE in what we do for our children, and for what our children endure.<br /><br />Symmetry Neuro-PT is a neurofeedback practice. One can only imagine how much much money they charge families to work with their child&#39;s different ability to make it a better kind of different ability. Almost as if it&#39;s a disability.<br /><br /><a href="https://twitter.com/ageofautism" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Follow us on Twitter</a><br /><br />COMMENTS FROM <a href="https://www.facebook.com/AgeofAutism/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">FACEBOOK</a></p>\r\n<p>I just showed this to my daughter, 35 years old, autistic who said, it\xe2\x80\x99s a disability all right. Which is why she\xe2\x80\x99s still at home and will never work. If that\xe2\x80\x99s not a disability I don\xe2\x80\x99t know what is.</p>\r\n<p>It\xe2\x80\x99s just a different ability, that\xe2\x80\x99s why my 28yo daughter needs 24/7 care. Hitting herself and others isn\xe2\x80\x99t a disability? Come on over to my house!</p>\r\n\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t    <p class="entry-more-link font-entrybody"><a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/twitter-disagreement-autism-is-a-disability-not-just-a-difference.html#more">Continue reading "Twitter Disagreement Autism Is a Disability Not Just a Difference" &raquo;</a></p>\n                        \n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a fa-facebook"></i></a>\n     \n</span>\n\t</p>\n\n\n</div>\n\n\n</article>\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\n    \n\n\n\n\n<!-- entry shared -->\n\n<article class="post entry">\n\n\n\n<!-- DISPLAY FULL POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/part-2-frau-komas-second-coming-mass-murder-autism-and-the-cult-of-weaponized-genetics.html">Part 2: Frau Koma\'s Second Coming: Mass Murder, Autism and the Cult of Weaponized Genetics</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e2017d3fe24db0970c-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="Frau K By Adriana Gamondes" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e2017d3fe24db0970c img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e2017d3fe24db0970c-400wi" style="width: 400px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="Frau K By Adriana Gamondes" /></a> Part 2 of Adriana Gamondes&#39; opus on school shooters that first ran several years ago. Alas, the topic is evergreen and growing ever greener.<br /><strong><br />Part 2, Profectus <br /><br />Read <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2013/01/frau-komas-second-coming-mass-murder-autism-and-the-cult-of-weaponized-genetics.html" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Part 1</a> and <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2013/01/part-3-frau-komas-second-coming-mass-murder-autism-and-the-cult-of-weaponized-genetics-.html" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Part 3</a>.</strong></p>\r\n<p><em>&quot;No wonder kids grow up crazy. A cat&#39;s cradle is nothing but a bunch of X&#39;s between somebody&#39;s hands, and little kids look and look and look at all those X&#39;s...&quot;<br />&quot;And?&quot;</em><br /><em>&quot;No damn cat, and no damn cradle.&quot; ~</em>Kurt Vonnegut<em>, Cat\xe2\x80\x99s Cradle</em></p>\r\n<p>By Adriana Gamondes</p>\r\n<p>In the introduction to <em>Nuclear Rites</em>, Stanford anthropologist Hugh Gusterson explains why he approached a formal study of atomic weapons scientists in the same manner he\xe2\x80\x99d approach a tribal culture: \xe2\x80\x9cone powerful Western institution that is particularly understudied by anthropologists is science.\xe2\x80\x9d</p>\r\n<p>Gusterson concludes that, though typical psychological analyses of weapons production bear some truth\xe2\x80\x94that the power of nuclear weapons systems become an extension of the self, an expression of potency,etc.\xe2\x80\x94the view too easily dismisses scientists\xe2\x80\x99 own rationalizations and ideology as mere distractions from driving psychosexual motives. Instead, according to Gusterson, scientists\xe2\x80\x99 faith in the ultimate morality of their work and the fact that this stems from the problems they\xe2\x80\x99re charged with solving (namely the belief that winning the arms race would prevent nuclear strikes by less evolved nations) might better explain the field\xe2\x80\x99s&#0160; euphemization of risks,&#0160; romanticization of their technology and exaggerated self-assurance that this technology can be controlled even in the face of repeated <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_military_nuclear_accidents" rel="noopener" target="_blank">human error and equipment malfunction</a> &#0160;potentially costing the lives of millions. Gusterson discusses profit mostly as it pertains to scientific status, coveted name-rights and the ritual of \xe2\x80\x9cinitiation and transcendence\xe2\x80\x9d involved in creation and testing.</p>\r\n<p>The word \xe2\x80\x9cprofit\xe2\x80\x9d is derived from the Latin profectus\xe2\x80\x94\xe2\x80\x9cto gain, advance or progress.\xe2\x80\x9c There are a variety of interweaving gains to be made in ventures that are perceived to advance humanity in the name of progress\xe2\x80\x94money is only one of them. Gusterson quotes <em>Robert Budwine, h</em>ead of the USA Delegation and director of Lawrence Livermore Laboratory:</p>\r\n<p><em>The United States, for all our manifest faults, is without a doubt the best hope for a future world of peace and prosperity\xe2\x80\xa6 Weapons research simply must continue at a determined and intensive level for our nation to have the opportunity to lead humankind towards some future utopian world order.</em></p>\r\n<p>Several of Gusterson\xe2\x80\x99s works begin with a quote from E.L. Doctorow: \xe2\x80\x9cThe bomb first was our weapon. Then it became our diplomacy. Next it became our economy. Now it\xe2\x80\x99s become our culture. We\xe2\x80\x99ve become the people of the bomb.\xe2\x80\x9d</p>\r\n<p>\xe2\x80\x9cTo the victor go the spoils\xe2\x80\x9d has a different meaning in that sense. Gusterson also points out in <a href="https://www.amazon.com/Insecure-American-Here-Should-About/dp/0520259718" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><em>The Insecure American</em></a> that by becoming terrifying on the path to progress\xe2\x80\x94even if this is rationalized, as it always has been, as the conscious pursuit of the \xe2\x80\x9cgreater good\xe2\x80\x9d\xe2\x80\x94we\xe2\x80\x99ve terrified ourselves. Fear sells, but we\xe2\x80\x99re the chief consumers of it.</p>\r\n<p>Every social policy which requires the cover of morality and pursuit of a shining future to rationalize human and ecological collateral is now framed as a \xe2\x80\x9cwar\xe2\x80\x9d on some frightening specter or other: the war on terror, the war on disease, the war on street drugs, and the war on mental illness (providing the sanctioned replacement for street drugs).&#0160; Some are beginning to recognize that whenever the \xe2\x80\x9cwar on\xe2\x80\x9d prefix is attached to any problem, whatever the \xe2\x80\x9cwar\xe2\x80\x9d has been declared on will expand.</p>\r\n<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="http://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e2017d3fe2518d970c-pi" style="display: inline;"><img alt="AG War on Ed" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e2017d3fe2518d970c" src="http://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e2017d3fe2518d970c-400wi" style="width: 400px;" title="AG War on Ed" /></a><br /><br /></p>\r\n<p>The voting public might backlash against some of these proverbial wars (case in point, the legalization of recreational marijuana in two states), but public opinion is increasingly feeble when it comes up against corporate interests. Most American voters wanted withdrawal from Afghanistan and for Wall Street bankers to be held accountable. Many were repelled by the Supreme Court\xe2\x80\x99s decision to gut limits on corporate campaign financing and <a href="http://www2.med.umich.edu/prmc/media/newsroom/details.cfm?ID=1760" rel="noopener" target="_blank">almost 90% of Americans are concerned about vaccine and prescription drug safety</a>. But as clinical psychologist Bruce Levine wrote in a <em>Huffington Post</em> article entitled <a href="http://www.huffingtonpost.com/bruce-e-levine/the-myth-of-us-democracy-corporatocracy_b_836573.html"><em>The Myth of U.S. Democracy and the Reality of U.S. Corporatocracy</em></a>, \xe2\x80\x9c\xe2\x80\x99We the People\xe2\x80\x99 have zero impact on policy.\xe2\x80\x9d</p>\r\n\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t    <p class="entry-more-link font-entrybody"><a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/part-2-frau-komas-second-coming-mass-murder-autism-and-the-cult-of-weaponized-genetics.html#more">Continue reading "Part 2: Frau Koma\'s Second Coming: Mass Murder, Autism and the Cult of Weaponized Genetics" &raquo;</a></p>\n                        \n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" href="https://profile.typepad.com/rescuepost">Age of Autism</a> on June 07, 2022 at 06:00 AM in <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/setting-goals.html">Setting Goals</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202942fae42b4200c-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="Setting goals" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202942fae42b4200c img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202942fae42b4200c-250wi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="Setting goals" /></a>I goofed on Sunday and set this post for 6:00pm instead of am! So Cathy missed much of the day, and I&#39;m sure readers missed her. Call it Senioritis on my part, the old age kind. So sorry!&#0160; Enjoy Cathy on a Monday. Tomorrow, Frau Koma Part 2 - as we look into school violence in Adriana Gamondes&#39; chilling three part essay. Thanks.<br /><br />By Cathy Jameson<br /><br />One of the contacts we have with one of Ronan\xe2\x80\x99s program called last week.&#0160; She needed to go over some paperwork that gets reviewed and refiled yearly.&#0160; I don\xe2\x80\x99t usually dread the conversation I have with her like I do when some other people call.&#0160; For the most part, it\xe2\x80\x99s simple stuff that she asks about.&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;</p>\r\n<p><em>How\xe2\x80\x99s he doing?&#0160; </em></p>\r\n<p><em>Any changes in his health or development?</em></p>\r\n<p><em>Any hospitalizations or E.R. admits in the last 3 months?</em></p>\r\n<p><em>Any problems with medications?</em></p>\r\n<p>After she asks those questions, we then review goals.&#0160; I <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2018/03/coordinated-care.html" rel="noopener" target="_blank">was stunned the first time</a> she\xe2\x80\x99d asked me to make a year-long goal when we enrolled in the program.&#0160; Goals had always been something we created with therapists and educators, never with medical personnel.&#0160; I\xe2\x80\x99d forgotten about this portion of the call and was again taken aback when she asked which new goals I wanted to make.&#0160;</p>\r\n<p>\xe2\x80\x9cGoals?&#0160; Hmmm, I can think of a few, but remind me what I said last time,\xe2\x80\x9d I replied.</p>\r\n<p><em>To become more actively engaged in community outings</em></p>\r\n<p>I laughed.&#0160; I laughed so hard.&#0160; Then I said, \xe2\x80\x98The covid lockdown, and then the shuttering of places we\xe2\x80\x99d normally go, shot down any chance of creating meaningful outings.&#0160; By the time places were open again, Ronan was so out of his normal routine.&#0160; He didn\xe2\x80\x99t want to go anywhere or do any of the usual things he used to do.&#0160; He still doesn\xe2\x80\x99t some days.&#0160; We try to get him interested in things, including stuff his siblings are doing like we\xe2\x80\x99ve always done, but it\xe2\x80\x99s been a struggle.\xe2\x80\x9d</p>\r\n<p>The nurse completely understood.</p>\r\n\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t    <p class="entry-more-link font-entrybody"><a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/setting-goals.html#more">Continue reading "Setting Goals" &raquo;</a></p>\n                        \n\n\n\n\n\n<hr </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202942fae2c4f200c-pi"><img alt="Inclusion" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202942fae2c4f200c img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202942fae2c4f200c-300wi" style="width: 281px; display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="Inclusion" /></a><br /><em>Florida threatened to fine Special Olympics International $27.5 million for requiring 5,500 participants at the <a href="https://www.orlandosentinel.com/coronavirus/os-ne-special-olympics-games-covid-vaccine-controversy-20220513-nbog6kwytndarewfdvp22ka5u4-story.html">USA Games in Orlando to be vaccinated against COVID,</a> prompting the organization to drop the mandate.</em></p>\r\n<p><em>\xe2\x80\x9cThere needs to be a choice in this regard,\xe2\x80\x9d Gov. Ron DeSantis said at an event in Orlando surrounded by a cheering crowd that included athletes for the games set to begin Sunday. \xe2\x80\x9cLet them compete. We want everyone to be able to compete.\xe2\x80\x9d&#0160; <a href="https://www.orlandosentinel.com/politics/os-ne-desantis-special-olympics-vaccine-20220603-aelfx7d6ijamrbm2i7jqoqxxaa-story.html" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Read more at Orlando Sentinel</a></em><br /><br />###<br /><br />AMEN. You should not be able claim to be an organization that welcomes all athletes with special needs and turn away HEALTHY athletes due to their vaccination status. Not for Covid, not for anything. Better to order and pay for titre and antibody tests for every single athlete before every single event.&#0160; See how many participate then.&#0160; Good job, Florida.</p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\n\t\t\t\n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/autism-prevalence-since-2000-wayne-rohde-interviews-dr-walter-zahorodny.html">Autism Prevalence Since 2000: Wayne Rohde Interviews Dr. Walter Zahorodny</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><span class="asset  asset-video at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202942fade8ef200c img-responsive"><a href="https://www.rescuepost.com/files/walter-zahorodony---audio.mp4"> </a><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e2027880803a3c200d-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="Increase" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e2027880803a3c200d img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e2027880803a3c200d-250wi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="Increase" /></a><a href="https://www.rescuepost.com/files/walter-zahrodony---audio.mp4">Download Walter Zahorodony - audio</a><br /><br /><span class="asset  asset-generic at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202788080725e200d img-responsive"><a href="https://www.rescuepost.com/files/walter-zahorodny-interview.pdf">Download Walter Zahorodny interview</a></span></span><br /><br />By Anne Dachel</p>\r\n<p>The audio link above is to an interview by Wayne Rohde who produces the Right on Point podcast and the Autism File podcast, with <a href="https://njms-web.njms.rutgers.edu/profile/myProfile.php?mbmid=zahorodn" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Dr. Walter Zahorodny.</a> <br />Dr. Zahorodny is the Research Director of the NJ Autism Study,&#0160; and has been studying the prevalence of autism since 2000. He was very open about what autism is doing to our children. He\xe2\x80\x99s been watching the increases for more than 20 years, and he\xe2\x80\x99s the first to tell us that they are real. More children actually have autism and something in the environment is causing it. He also makes it clear that the future is very dark because the numbers show no signs of slowing down.</p>\r\n<p>I transcribed the entire interview, highlighting in bold the most noteworthy statements.</p>\r\n<p>It\xe2\x80\x99s impossible to dismiss the statistics and facts that Zahorodny cites here, yet the Centers for Disease Control and Prevention have been doing just that for the last several decades. In fact, he describes the underhanded methods in play by the CDC to underestimate just how bad the increases are with the DSM-5 and what Zahorodny refers to as ADDM TWO.</p>\r\n<p><strong><em>The most recent CDC report, the one that reports on study year 2018, is very interesting in that for the first time, they\xe2\x80\x99re not really concerned with autism prevalence. They\xe2\x80\x99re not really reporting. If you read carefully, you\xe2\x80\x99ll find out that they changed the methodology, and they\xe2\x80\x99re not really concern with what is the true prevalence of autism.</em></strong></p>\r\n<p><strong><em>One thing that maybe nobody understands, maybe through your podcast people will begin to appreciate the fact that the CDC no longer\xe2\x80\x94and the ADDM Network\xe2\x80\x94no longer does active population surveillance. </em></strong></p>\r\n<p><strong><em>We\xe2\x80\x99re not trying to find all the cases of autism. That\xe2\x80\x99s the old system. I would call the old system ADDM ONE. You\xe2\x80\x99re trying to find all the true cases. </em></strong></p>\r\n<p>Zahorodny cites statistics that should cause panic in officials who get billions of dollars a year to oversee our health. Not only do the people at the CDC refuse to acknowledge that more children have autism, but they\xe2\x80\x99ve successfully covered up the real rate of autism.</p>\r\n\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t    <p class="entry-more-link font-entrybody"><a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/autism-prevalence-since-2000-wayne-rohde-interviews-dr-walter-zahorodny.html#more">Continue reading "Autism Prevalence Since 2000: Wayne Rohde Interviews Dr. Walter Zahorodny" &raquo;</a></p>\n                        \n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info    \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/best-of-frau-koma-returns-after-yet-another-mass-shooting.html">Best Of: Frau Koma Returns After Yet Another Mass Shooting</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><strong> <a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e2017ee733082c970d-pi"><img alt="Frau K By Adriana Gamondes" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e2017ee733082c970d img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e2017ee733082c970d-400wi" style="width: 400px; display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="Frau K By Adriana Gamondes" /></a><br /><br /></strong>Note: Yes. Again.Adriana Gamondes wrote this searing three part post several years ago. She had a style that could not compare. Unfortunately, we have to recycle it as mass shootings have worsened. If any readers have been in contact with Adriana, please let us know, we have tried to reach her.&#0160; Thanks.<strong><br /><br /></strong><em>\xe2\x80\x9cKoma\xe2\x80\x9c is \xe2\x80\x9camok\xe2\x80\x9d spelled backwards; amok\xe2\x80\x94as in \xe2\x80\x9cto run amok.\xe2\x80\x9d \xe2\x80\x9cAmoklaufen\xe2\x80\x9d is the German expression for \xe2\x80\x9cspree-killer.\xe2\x80\x9d After a mass shooting at the <a href="http://www.drossmann.de/wordpress/2009/09/30/german-school-shootings-1-robert-steinhaeuser-erfurt-2002-in-a-nutshell/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Johannes Gutenberg Gymnasium</a> in Erfurt, Eastern Germany in 2002, police developed a new emergency code for school shootings\xe2\x80\x94\xe2\x80\x9cFrau Koma kommt\xe2\x80\x9d\xe2\x80\x94\xe2\x80\x9cFrau Koma is coming.\xe2\x80\x9d</em><br /><strong><br />Part 1, &#0160;Demon Seed <br /></strong></p>\r\n<p><em>And death and hell were cast into the lake of fire. This is the second death. And whosoever was not found written in the book of life was cast into the lake of fire. &#0160;~Revelations, 20:14-15</em></p>\r\n<p>By Adriana Gamondes</p>\r\n<p>In September, 2011, Manitoba judge Robert Heinrichs ruled that a <a href="http://ssristories.com/show.php?item=5155" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">sixteen year old accused of murder</a> would remain in youth court where he faces a maximum sentence of four years rather than the possibility of life without parole in adult court. Family members of the fifteen year old victim were outraged by the ruling, though Heinrichs stated that the accused\xe2\x80\x99s<strong> \xe2\x80\x9c</strong>basic normalcy now further confirms he no longer poses a risk of violence to anyone and that his mental deterioration and resulting violence would not have taken place without exposure to Prozac\xe2\x80\xa6He has none of the characteristics of a perpetrator of violence.\xe2\x80\x9d</p>\r\n<p>Dr. Peter Breggin, the reform psychiatrist and psychopharmaceutical expert who testified on antidepressant-induced psychosis and violence in the Manitoba case, was sued for his medical license in 1987\xe2\x80\x94the very year that Prozac was first mass marketed by Eli Lilly. The <a href="https://www.nytimes.com/1987/09/22/science/free-expression-or-irresponsibility-psychiatrist-faces-a-hearing-today.html?sec=health" rel="noopener" target="_blank">charges</a> were filed by the National Alliance on Mental Illness (NAMI), a consumer group which has always lobbied for forced institutionalization and mandated treatment of the mentally ill ( <a href="http://www.nami.org/Template.cfm?section=NAMI_Policy_Platform&amp;Template=/ContentManagement/ContentDisplay.cfm&amp;ContentID=38245" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Section 9.2</a> of NAMI\xe2\x80\x99s Public Policy Platform)\xe2\x80\x94including drugs and electroconvulsive therapy or <a href="http://www.nami.org/Template.cfm?Section=About_Treatments_and_Supports&amp;Template=/ContentManagement/ContentDisplay.cfm&amp;ContentID=142939" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">ECT</a>\xe2\x80\x94 and was recently exposed as a long-standing pharmaceutical industry front organization in <a href="https://www.nytimes.com/2009/10/22/health/22nami.html" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank"><em>The New York Times</em></a>.</p>\r\n<p>Due to his success in banning forced lobotomy in institutions coupled with efforts to raise the alarm on clinical risks of ECT and psychiatric drugs, Dr. Breggin has been a thorn in the side of industry and its various front organizations since the 1970\xe2\x80\x99s. After Breggin went on <em>Oprah</em> and reported that Eli Lilly\xe2\x80\x99s own trial data showed that even individuals lacking histories of violence or serious mental illness who were exposed to the Selective Serotonin Reuptake Inhibitor (SSRI) antidepressant Prozac and antipsychotics would frequently develop violent ideation or violent psychosis, NAMI claimed that Breggin\xe2\x80\x99s remarks could cause patients to discontinue their meds. Following an outpouring of support for Breggin from the international medical reform community, the Maryland licensure board dropped the charges and Breggin prevailed. Seventeen years later, the FDA adopted black box warnings for suicide and violence on SSRI antidepressants. The black box warnings are, almost word for word, the precise clinical caveats that Breggin repeatedly submitted to the FDA and in Congressional hearings.</p>\r\n<p>The previously concealed Prozac trial data Breggin uncovered and exposed in 1987 included cases of child subjects on Prozac who suddenly developed intrusive dreams and visions of going to school with guns and shooting classmates.&#0160; There were also far more attempted and completed suicides among drug-exposed subjects than in the placebo groups.</p>\r\n<p>Over the years, Breggin and other researchers have worked to identify the mechanism by which certain psychopharmaceutical drugs induce violence and suicidality. Breggin has described phenomenon such as <a href="https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pubmed/2574607" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">drug-induced akathisia</a>, an uncontrollable sense of restless inner torment caused by an amphetamine-like and even LSD-like effect of selective serotonin reuptake inhibitors or SSRI\xe2\x80\x99s, and has written about prescription drug-induced<strong> \xe2\x80\x9c</strong><a href="http://www.huffingtonpost.com/dr-peter-breggin/medication-madness-how-ps_b_223922.html" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">intoxication anosognosia</a>\xe2\x80\x9d or \xe2\x80\x9cmedication spellbinding<strong>: </strong></p>\r\n<p><em>Medication spellbinding has four basic effects. </em></p>\r\n\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t    <p class="entry-more-link font-entrybody"><a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/best-of-frau-koma-returns-after-yet-another-mass-shooting.html#more">Continue reading "Best Of: Frau Koma Returns After Yet Another Mass Shooting" &raquo;</a></p>\n                        \n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" href="https://profile.typepad.com/rescuepost">Age of Autism</a> on June 02, 2022 at 06:00 AM in <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/adriana-gamondes/">Adriana Gamondes</a> </span> <span class="separator">|</span> <a class="permalink" href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/best-of-frau-koma-returns-after-yet-another-mass-shooting.html">Permalink</a>\n\n \n\t<span class="separator"> \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/summer-breakation-and-autism.html">Summer Breakation and Autism</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<div class="photo-wrap photo-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202942fada23c200c" id="photo-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202942fada23c200c" style="float: left; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px; width: 250px;"><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202942fada23c200c-pi"><img alt="Retro school&#39;s out" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202942fada23c200c img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202942fada23c200c-250wi" style="width: 250px;" title="Retro school&#39;s out" /></a>\r\n<div class="photo-caption caption-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202942fada23c200c" id="caption-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202942fada23c200c">In September, for my youngest.</div>\r\n</div>\r\n<p>Extended School Year, or ESY, is a hot topic in special education. Programs vary dramatically from state to state and school district to school district.&#0160; Our town district ESY changed over the years, from 5 days a week, for 6 weeks to 4 days a week for a month, with a shortened day. My youngest is about to begin her final round of ESY at her private placement in July.&#0160; Hers is a 5 day program, and runs 4 weeks. There&#39;s a good 6 weeks of downtime. It&#39;s discouraging. Worse? She ages out of school altogether in September. As of now, there is no program that will accept her, because she has a gigantic budget that includes a 1:1. I say that tongue in cheek. Her state administered budget will sit, unused, unless a program that I deem acceptable will accept her. Even the program where her sisters attend is up in the air, because of the severe staffing shortage. Programs are more amenable to taking in 3:1 individuals.&#0160; Those who qualify for a 1:1 are being turned away - they are money losers.&#0160; ESY is looking pretty good to me. I know the staff, my daughter loves her school, and I&#39;m clinging to the last week weeks of programming like a liferaft<br /><br />Use the comments section to share your ESY experiences - good, bad or ugly.</p>\r\n<p>&#0160;</p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\n\t\t\t\n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" href="https://profile.typepad.com/rescuepost">Age of Autism</a> on June 01, 2022 at 06:00 AM in <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/current_affairs/">Current Affairs</a> </span> <span class="separator">|</span> <a class="permalink" href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/06/summer-breakation-and-autism.html">Permalink</a>\n\n \n\t<span class="separator"> | </span>\n\t\n\t\t\t <a class="entry-comments" \n</span>\n\t</p>\n\n\n</div>\n\n\n</article>\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\n    \n\n\n\n\n<!-- entry shared -->\n\n<article class="post entry">\n\n\n\n<!-- DISPLAY FULL POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/the-passing-years-since-the-age-of-autism-was-published-by-olmsted-blaxill.html">The Passing Years Since The Age of Autism Was Published By Olmsted & Blaxill</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202942fad5b5d200c-pi"><img alt="Mark and Dan at AO book debut" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202942fad5b5d200c img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202942fad5b5d200c-450wi" style="width: 450px; display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="Mark and Dan at AO book debut" /></a><br />Facebook should come with a box of tissues. Yesterday&#39;s memory was from 11 &#0160;years ago, when Mark Blaxill and Dan Olmsted shared advance copies of their book titled, <a href="https://www.amazon.com/Age-Autism-Medicine-Man-Made-Epidemic/dp/0312547099/ref=tmm_pap_swatch_0?_encoding=UTF8&amp;qid=&amp;sr=" rel="noopener" target="_blank">The Age of Autism Mercury Medicine and a Manmade Epidemic </a>at Autism One. Dan has been gone for 5 and a half years. <a href="https://obits.ocregister.com/us/obituaries/orangecounty/name/edmund-arranga-obituary?id=31897892" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Ed Arranga passed away last December.</a>. (I hope that isn&#39;t springing the news on you.) This blog was launched by Dan and Mark in preparation for their book. Dan&#39;s life work became autism. After a stellar journalism career, he devoted himself to the epidemic. To a degree, we all abandonned our initial careers when autism broke into our homes. We were drafted. Dan enlisted. He provided a steady, guiding hand, and together he and Mark produced Pulitzer quality work that was often largely ignored or suppressed. Blogs ruled the landscape, and we had intense rivalries, that, looking back, seem quaint. HeraldBlog, Orac, Kristina Chew, Kevin Leitch, Amanda Baggs - how they dined on us in their never ending effort to make sure no one believed in the autism epidemic. <br /><br />Last week, the United States was pummeled by another school shooting. 19 schoolkids, 2 teachers, 1 husband who could not bear the grief. Another epidemic that seems to have no resolution even when its carnage can not be denied. It&#39;s tough to gaslight families when there are corpses. A Facebook commenter made a reference to something Dr. Bernard Rimland may have said or written, about a generation of angry boys growing up.&#0160; If you have the reference, let me know. It seems to be real.<br /><br /><br /></p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\n\t\t\t\n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" href="https://profile.typepad.com/rescuepost">Age of Autism</a> on May 31, 2022 at 06:00 AM in <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/current_affairs/">Current Affairs</a> </span> <span class="separator">|</span> <a class="permalink" href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/the-passing-years-since-the-age-of-autism-was-published-by-olmsted-blaxill.html">Permalink</a>\n\n \n\t<span class="separator"> | </span>\n\t\n\t\t\t <a POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/commemorating-memorial-day.html">Commemorating Memorial Day</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202942fad3bc4200c-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="CD2956A5-68B2-45FE-987E-D98336DA7711" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202942fad3bc4200c img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202942fad3bc4200c-250wi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="CD2956A5-68B2-45FE-987E-D98336DA7711" /></a>I\xe2\x80\x99ve been trying to explain Memorial Day to my daughter. So far, she\xe2\x80\x99s grabbed onto \xe2\x80\x9c\xe2\x80\xa6war, people died.\xe2\x80\x9d It\xe2\x80\x99s a better grasp than mattress sales and potato salad to start the Summer. How do you explain the concept of death. Of war. Of life as it stands today, to a pure soul like our kids?</p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\n\t\t\t\n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info \n</span>\n\t</p>\n\n\n</div>\n\n\n</article>\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\n    \n\n\n\n\n<!-- entry shared -->\n\n<article class="post entry">\n\n\n\n<!-- DISPLAY FULL POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/always-something.html"> Always Something</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202942fad16eb200c-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="It&#39;s always something" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202942fad16eb200c img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202942fad16eb200c-250wi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="It&#39;s always something" /></a>By Cathy Jameson</p>\r\n<p><em>When one has as many kids and as busy a schedule as we have, the expression, \xe2\x80\x9cThere\xe2\x80\x99s always something going on!\xe2\x80\x9d perfectly sums up our life.&#0160; That expression rings through once more\xe2\x80\xa6and makes for some interesting (and maybe even entertaining) storytelling here.&#0160; </em></p>\r\n<p>Two weeks ago, a hornet crawled out of a floor vent in our den.&#0160; Ronan\xe2\x80\x99s caregiver was home with Ronan when the scary, flying beast emerged.&#0160; She trapped it, God bless her, and was rightly traumatized afterwards from the frightening few minutes the hornet was in my home.&#0160;</p>\r\n<p>Later, while telling my husband about the incident, he said it might be time to call an exterminator.&#0160; We\xe2\x80\x99d seen wasps in the house when the weather had started to warm up.&#0160; A friend in the area had shared that they, too, get wasps in the house \xe2\x80\x93 sometimes from their chimney, sometimes through an air vent.&#0160; Like the friend does, I trap and kill them.&#0160; I used to be a catch-and-release kinda gal.&#0160; Not so much anymore.&#0160; I like nature, but I never like to see that sort of nature in my house.&#0160; Unable to figure out how these insects were coming in, I knew we had to do something more.&#0160;</p>\r\n<p>A few exterminator companies would be available to help me, but I know that their first-line of defense would sometimes be some sort of chemical concoction.&#0160; I didn\xe2\x80\x99t want that option in case whatever they used would have negative interactions with Ronan\xe2\x80\x99s health.&#0160; After speaking to the company\xe2\x80\x99s representative, who completely understood my predicament (and who said she\xe2\x80\x99d be living in a hotel room if she ever experienced a hornet in the house), I agreed to have their technician come over for an inspection.&#0160; I\xe2\x80\x99d have to wait a few days though.&#0160; Their schedule and mine wouldn\xe2\x80\x99t match up until after the weekend.</p>\r\n<p>While I anxiously waited, Ronan\xe2\x80\x99s big sister helped put screens over every floor vent in the house.&#0160; It might be a temporary fix, we said, but it was one that made our adrenaline rush less.&#0160;</p>\r\n<p>I got up early Monday morning to make breakfast for Ronan before woke up and to be ready for the inspection.&#0160; Hoping he\xe2\x80\x99d sleep in since he\xe2\x80\x99d had two very early morning wake ups two days in a row, Ronan decided that the very second the technician drove down our driveway would be the very best time to wake up.&#0160; He didn\xe2\x80\x99t come find me right away like he usually does after waking up, but waited a few minutes.&#0160; I was glad for that because it gave me a few minutes to give the young tech some information about the hornet that scared us.&#0160;</p>\r\n<p>While the tech was telling me what he would do first, which would be a walkthrough of the house and a peek in the attic, I heard Ronan walking toward us.&#0160; So as not to startle the young man, I said, \xe2\x80\x9cOh, hey, there\xe2\x80\x99s my son.\xe2\x80\x9d&#0160; The young man replied, \xe2\x80\x9cYes, I heard you had a son that has some medical conditions and that you\xe2\x80\x99re concerned with some of the sprays used to treat bugs.\xe2\x80\x9d&#0160; As I gave him a quick rundown of my concerns, Ronan took himself to the bathroom.&#0160; Within a few seconds, I could hear that he was actually using the bathroom.</p>\r\n<p><em>Wow, </em>I thought<em>, great job, Rone!&#0160; All those mornings that we, or his caregiver, had guided him to the bathroom first thing in the morning is paying off.&#0160; </em></p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t    <p class="entry-more-link font-entrybody"><a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/always-something.html#more">Continue reading " Always Something" &raquo;</a></p>\n                        \n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" href="https://profile.typepad.com/rescuepost">Age of Autism</a> on May 29, 2022 at 06:00 AM in <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/cathy-jameson/">Cathy Jameson</a> </span> <span \n</span>\n\t</p>\n\n\n</div>\n\n\n</article>\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\n    \n\n\n\n\n<!-- entry shared -->\n\n<article class="post entry">\n\n\n\n<!-- DISPLAY FULL POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/safeminds-new-study-shows-1-in-100-children-are-diagnosed-with-asd-around-the-world.html">Safeminds: New Study Shows 1 in 100 Children Are Diagnosed with ASD Around the World</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a href="https://safeminds.org/news/its-not-just-the-u-s-global-autism-rates-continue-to-climb/" rel="noopener" target="_blank"> </a><strong><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e20278807f4d04200d-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="Lather rinse repeat" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e20278807f4d04200d img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e20278807f4d04200d-200wi" style="width: 200px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="Lather rinse repeat" /></a></strong>Below is a new article from <a href="https://safeminds.org/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Safeminds</a>.&#0160; Familiar name Andy Shih says, &quot;Efforts at awareness are succeeding.&quot; Awareness is a dirty word by now in the USA, but elsewhere in the world, there is a huge need to educate. I recently worked with a Mom in Ethiopia, whose 7 year old has been diagnosed. The stigma and ignorance were severe. Thanks to TACA and NAA, we were able to send helpful materials to her. <br /><br />###<strong><br /><br /><a href="https://safeminds.org/news/its-not-just-the-u-s-global-autism-rates-continue-to-climb/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">New Study Shows 1 in 100 Children Are Diagnosed with ASD Around the World</a></strong></p>\r\n<p>Recent research shows approximately 100 in 10,000 \xe2\x80\x93 or 1 in 100 \xe2\x80\x93 children across the globe hold an autism diagnosis. This figure comes from a new systematic review of 99 prevalence estimates from 34 countries.&#0160; A <a href="https://onlinelibrary.wiley.com/doi/10.1002/aur.239">decade ago</a>, the global rate was 62 in 10,000. Similar to the U.S., the study found that boys worldwide are four times more likely than girls to have autism. Also included in the study was the median percentage of autism with co-occurring intellectual disability, which was reported at 33%. The studies analyzed for the review varied in size, ranging from 465 participants to 50 million. The prevalence estimates also varied greatly, ranging from 1.09 in 10,000 to 436 in 10,000. Most of the studies included in the review were conducted in the U.S. and Northern Europe. However, previously underrepresented regions like Africa and the Middle East were also included. The study\xe2\x80\x99s lead author, Andy Shih, suggests that these findings show efforts to improve autism awareness are succeeding and that many regions have improved in identifying, diagnosing, and treating individuals with autism. Shih also believes the rise in the new global autism rate is due to changes in the definition of autism and differences in the methodology and contexts of prevalence studies.</p>\r\n<p><a href="https://www.disabilityscoop.com/2022/05/19/autism-prevalence-rising-globally/29864/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Original Article</a></p>\r\n<p><a href="https://onlinelibrary.wiley.com/doi/full/10.1002/aur.2696" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Original Study</a></p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\n\t\t\t\n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" href="https://profile.typepad.com/rescuepost">Age of Autism</a> on POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/180-x-6-x-13.html">180 x 6 x 13</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202942facdad6200c-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="Salvador ramos" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202942facdad6200c img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202942facdad6200c-250wi" style="width: 212px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="Salvador ramos" /></a>180 school days x 6 hours a day x 13 years (K-12) = 14,040 hours in the care of professional teachers, therapists, social workers, school psychologists, administrators and surrounded by peers.<br /><br />WHAT. GOES. SO. WRONG?<br /><br />Here in Connecticut, we are still dealing with the aftermath of a stabbing at a high school party two weeks ago. One teen named <a href="https://www.courant.com/news/connecticut/hc-news-friends-family-community-mourn-james-mcgrath-20220521-22x4dojkvrayxexrxhgoujoipi-story.html" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Jimmy McGrath</a> was killed, three injured, and the aggressor, a 16 year old student, is out on a $2,000,000 bond awaiting trial as an adult. <br /><br />I can&#39;t bring myself to call these young men monsters - though their actions are monstrous. They aren&#39;t serial killers like Jeffrey Dahmer, who can be profiled back to childhood with violent fascinations. I cringe when I hear in almost every case, &quot;He was a loner. He didn&#39;t talk to anyone. He had no friends. He dressed weird.&#0160; He kept to himself.&quot;&#0160; <br /><br />I suppose will we learn bits and pieces, while the media politicizes most of the tragedy. </p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\n\t\t\t\n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" \n</span>\n\t</p>\n\n\n</div>\n\n\n</article>\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\n    \n\n\n\n\n<!-- entry shared -->\n\n<article class="post entry">\n\n\n\n<!-- DISPLAY FULL POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/would-kids-with-autism-survive-a-shooter.html">Would Kids With Autism Survive A Shooter?</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202942facc449200c-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="Go Talk Quiet" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202942facc449200c img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202942facc449200c-250wi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="Go Talk Quiet" /></a>The nation reels from another mass shooting at an elementary school. While listening to news reports throughout the day, I remembered something that happened to me several years ago. I was at the High School for one of my daughters&#39; IEP meetings. I was in the classroom with students and staff, including paras. Suddenly an alarm went off and an Active Shooter Drill was underway. I was closed in the classroom with everyone. None of the students with autism was completely quiet, including my daughter. One student was loud. Could have been any of my 3 daughters, none of whom can regulate their voice or stimming for more than a few seconds. One Paraprofessional asked, &quot;How would you keep him quiet,&quot; to the other. &quot;Oh, I&#39;d find a way to shut him up.&quot; I was appalled. But I know that if there were a situation like the massacre in Uvalde, Texas, or up the road from me in Newtown, Connecticut, some, many, most or perhaps all of the students with autism would be in grave danger because of their disability. This might be the ONLY time a quiet/seclusion room would be useful. I would like to think that most staff would try to shield the kids and keep them quiet. I&#39;m not sure I could keep my own kids quiet. And so I ask, if there is a shooter in a school, what happens to the special needs/autistic students, and is there a plan just for them that honors their needs?<br /><br /></p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\n\t\t\t\n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" href="https://profile.typepad.com/rescuepost">Age of Autism</a> on May 26, 2022 at 06:00 AM in <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/nightmares/">Nightmares</a> </span> <span class="separator">|</span> <a class="permalink" href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/would-kids-with-autism-survive-a-shooter.html">Permalink</a>\n\n \n\t<span class="separator"> | </span>\n\t\n\t\t\t <a class="entry-comments" href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/would-kids-with-autism-survive-a-shooter.html#comments">Comments (6)</a>\n\t\n\n\n          </p>\n\n\n          <!-- technorati tags -->\n\n\n\n          <!-- post footer links -->\n\t<p class="entry-footer-share entry-footer-share-buttons">\n\t\t<span class="entry-footer-links-twitter">\n     <a
