target="_blank"><i class="icon fab fa-twitter"></i></a>\n</span> <span class="separator">|</span> <span class="entry-footer-links-plusone"></span> <span class="separator">|</span> <span class="entry-footer-links-pinterest">\n     <a href="javascript:void((function()%7Bvar%20e=document.createElement(\'script\');e.setAttribute(\'type\',\'text/javascript\');e.setAttribute(\'charset\',\'UTF-8\');e.setAttribute(\'src\',\'https://assets.pinterest.com/js/pinmarklet.js?r=\'+Math.random()*99999999);document.body.appendChild(e)%7D)());"><i class="icon fab fa-pinterest"></i></a>\n\n</span> <span class="separator">|</span> <span class="entry-footer-links-facebook_like">\n     \n     <a href="https://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.ageofautism.com%2F2022%2F05%2Fwould-kids-with-autism-survive-a-shooter.html" target="_blank"><i class="icon fab fa-facebook"></i></a>\n     \n</span>\n\t</p>\n\n\n</div>\n\n\n</article>\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n<!-- entry shared -->\n\n<article class="post entry">\n\n\n\n<!-- DISPLAY FULL POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/fractured-fairytales.html">Fractured Fairytales</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e20282e15765b0200b-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="Fractured fairy tales" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e20282e15765b0200b img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e20282e15765b0200b-250wi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="Fractured fairy tales" /></a>After I wrote this post, the news broke about 18 year old Salvador Ramos, who killed in cold blood 19 elementary school students and 2 adults in Uvalde, Texas. I am in no way equating the agony of having your child murdered in school with having a child with autism. I am going to point out that systems everywhere are broken beyond repair. And failing children right into adulthood. Those who make it. We have a generation that literally has the WORLD in their palm of their hand, and yet are so very alone. Angry. Vindictive. Without coping skills. We say it&#39;s a gun issue. We say it&#39;s a mental health issue. It seems like a radically altered childhood issue. And no one wants to talk about it. What the hell has happened to our kids?&#0160; <br /><br />###<br /><br />Those readers of a certain age will remember the Fractured Fairy Tales cartoons that aired during Bullwinkle. Today&#39;s post is about the fracturing within our community. Ignored. Disregarded. Glossed over. Not here.<br /><br />Many of our readers are drowning in ever deeper waters as their children head into adulthood. There are few supports once school lets out. Day programs are turning down autistic individuals with high levels of need.&#0160; Jobs are grim for those who qualify for viable employment with or without supports.&#0160; Medical freedom and Covid have eclipsed autism everywhere - even within organizations that were founded by warrior families. Biomedical treatment is a distant memory. Spelling has become the new darling.&#0160; New reports of beautiful Elizabeth Bonker, who was Valedictorian for her college class, they mention, &quot;She lost her speech at 15 months,&quot; but none asked WHY??? It&#39;s as if they said, &quot;She got glasses in 3rd grade.&quot; Perfectly normal. Spelling is wonderful, I&#39;ve seen my own daughters intelligence shine through. I am a big fan.&#0160; Then reality steps in. I just saw a spelling training program that sounds fantastic. 8 weeks of intensive training with support. $1000 per trainee. I need 4 or 5 trainees at least. I can&#39;t be the only &quot;voice&quot; for my 3 daughters. I need others to be able to train and learn, but at $1000 each? Even if I train them. Staff quits. What then? &#0160;I have been my daughters\xe2\x80\x99 &#0160;trainer for more than 25 years. And with spelling&#39;s success and marketing, there\xe2\x80\x99s yet another documentary, and an invitation to fly to the Midwest to view it. I&#0160; have a hard time getting to the Stop and Shop up the street. It&#39;s enough. If I sound like I&#39;m complaining, I am. I&#39;m angry that after 2+ decades of work, 15 years of Age of Autism, nothing much has changed for families. Young Moms who are able to get into a diagnosis center leave with exactly what most of us got years go. NOTHING. No road map. No plan. Just &quot;Call early intervention and find yourself 30 hours of ABA a week. Good luck, call us in a year.&quot; Students in school get speech and OT that are all but useless even after 18 years. Assistive Technology flopped, it&#39;s completely hit or miss who can use it, program it, buy an iPad every few months to replace the one thrown across the room and shattered. It&#39;s disheartening in the extreme. Yesterday, I saw a post that only hardened my heart. A dear friend of our community, a PhD with autism who was active at Autism One and other conferences, wrote <br /><br />&quot;<em><span class="d2edcug0 hpfvmrgz qv66sw1b c1et5uql lr9zc1uh a8c37x1j fe6kdd0r mau55g9w c8b282yb keod5gw0 nxhoafnm aigsh9s9 d3f4x2em iv3no6db jq4qci2q a3bd9o3v b1v8xokw oo9gr5id hzawbc8m" dir="auto">Reporting from London as XXX and I gear up to explore literature and research findings that support shifting to strength-based views of autistic people. We shall examine US and UK current models through a strength-based lens as we review advances in health, education, media and advocacy. What ideas do you have to shift from thinking of autism in terms of deficit, disability, and disorder toward abilities and strengths?</span><span class="d2edcug0 hpfvmrgz qv66sw1b c1et5uql lr9zc1uh a8c37x1j fe6kdd0r mau55g9w c8b282yb keod5gw0 nxhoafnm aigsh9s9 d3f4x2em iv3no6db jq4qci2q a3bd9o3v b1v8xokw oo9gr5id hzawbc8m" dir="auto">&quot; <br /><br /></span></em>My daughters will never travel to London. Lord, give me a &quot;strength based view,&quot; to keep going.&#0160; If you still love what we do at AofA - Anne, John, Cathy and I - we are AofA - please consider a donation to keep us going.&#0160; <br /><br />And to families in Uvalde, and in every city from coast to coast that has had a shooting, I&#39;m sorry we&#39;ve let our kids sink into this fractured fairy tale called the USA.<br /><br />Thanks.</p>\r\n<p>Kim</p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\n\t\t\t\n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/fractured-fairytales.html">Permalink</a>\n\n \n\t<span class="separator"> | </span>\n\t\n\t\t\t <a class="entry-comments" \n</span>\n\t</p>\n\n\n</div>\n\n\n</article>\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\n    \n\n\n\n\n<!-- entry shared -->\n\n<article class="post entry">\n\n\n\n<!-- DISPLAY FULL POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/autism-in-northern-ireland-we-cant-close-our-eyes-and-make-it-go-away.html">Autism In Northern Ireland: We Can\'t Close Our Eyes and Make It Go Away</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e20278807e9c48200d-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="Abadnonned school" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e20278807e9c48200d img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e20278807e9c48200d-250wi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="Abadnonned school" /></a>By Anne Dachel<br /><br />There\xe2\x80\x99s been another stunning announcement about autism in the UK. This time it\xe2\x80\x99s from Northern Ireland. An annual report released on May 20<sup>th</sup> revealed that, according to the Department of Health, <strong>one in every 17 students in the 6 counties of Northern Ireland is autistic. (</strong>This would also mean about one in every 10 boys.)</p>\r\n<p>Even more alarming are the numbers exclusively from Belfast. There one in every 14 students has a diagnosis.</p>\r\n<p>Here is the official report:<strong><a href="https://www.health-ni.gov.uk/sites/default/files/publications/health/asd-children-ni-2022.pdf" rel="noopener" target="_blank"> Prevalence of Autism (including Asperger Syndrome) in School&#0160; Age Children in Northern Ireland</a>.&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </strong></p>\r\n<p>This is what the BBC reported: <a href="https://www.bbc.com/news/uk-northern-ireland-61513905" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><strong>Autism: Proportion of NI pupils with diagnosis quadruples</strong></a> <a href="https://www.bbc.com/news/uk-northern-ireland-61513905"></a></p>\r\n<p><em>Boys were three times more likely to have a diagnosis of autism than girls</em></p>\r\n<p><em>The proportion of schoolchildren with an autism diagnosis in Northern Ireland has quadrupled in just over a decade, according to figures just published by the Department of Health.</em></p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t    <p class="entry-more-link font-entrybody"><a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/autism-in-northern-ireland-we-cant-close-our-eyes-and-make-it-go-away.html#more">Continue reading "Autism In Northern Ireland: We Can\'t Close Our Eyes and Make It Go Away" &raquo;</a></p>\n                        \n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" href="https://profile.typepad.com/rescuepost">Age of Autism</a> on May 24, 2022 at 06:00 AM in <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/media/">Anne Dachel</a> </span> <span class="separator">|</span> <a class="permalink" href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/autism-in-northern-ireland-we-cant-close-our-eyes-and-make-it-go-away.html">Permalink</a>\n\n \n\t<span    \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/harvard-sophomore-kristin-king-rails-against-violently-ableist-sadhguru-autism-awareness-panel.html">Harvard Sophomore Kristin King Rails Against Violently Ableist Sadhguru Autism Awareness Panel</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e20282e156e1de200b-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="Harvard ableist" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e20282e156e1de200b img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e20282e156e1de200b-250wi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="Harvard ableist" /></a>Here&#39;s the Cliff Notes version of Katie&#39;s perfectly pitched post: The &quot;#actuallyautistic nothing about us without us&quot; army is rabidly against our profoundly affected children. And institutions cower and collapse rather than FIGHT for our kids.&#0160;&#0160;<br /><br />We need to add the letter &quot;A&quot; to LGBTQRSTUVWXYZ and make sure our children&#39;s genitals are mentioned frequently to be on the cancel culture good list.&#0160; Maybe I&#39;ll dye my girls hair rainbow so that the likes of Kristin will notice them. Violently ableist.... Spend a day with one of our strapping adult males during an autistic episode and then talk to us about violence, Kristin.&#0160; The Ivory tower is actually made of cotton - and plugged into their deaf ears.<br /><br />###<br /><br />By Katie Wright:<br /><br />So many people hate the politically correct elitism of places like Harvard. But Harvard makes it so easy!!<br /><br />A few weeks ago, the Sadhguru Center, a TEACHING hospital associated with Harvard offered panel called, \xe2\x80\x9cAutism Awareness: Thinking Outside the Box.\xe2\x80\x9d It could not sound more innocuous.<br /><br />The panel described itself as a multidisciplinary discussion to explore autism beyond conventions. Sounds good to me. As a parent of a young man with severe autism, I have spent too much time educating doctors on the basics of autism. Apparently, they learn next to nothing about autism in medical school. Approximately 5% of American boys diagnosed with autism and almost half have chronic health problems.<br /><br />However, Harvard sophomore Kristin B. King went ballistic about the autism panel . This young woman claims to have autism. I know, I know......Lately, any smart, lonely, quirky, nonconformist labels themselves \xe2\x80\x9cautistic.\xe2\x80\x9d Almost none actually meet the DSM definition of autism. It is a disabling condition and makes communication and social interaction especially challenging. Not so for King! She rails against the conference, creates petitions to stop it, bullies Harvard administration.....I know, it\xe2\x80\x99s absurd.<br /><br />King declares, \xe2\x80\x9cOne of the panel\xe2\x80\x99s goals is to treat autism. That is not only violently ableist but scientifically incorrect!\xe2\x80\x9d Oh my God, King\xe2\x80\x99s histrionics make me wince with embarrassment for her. This is a bright young woman throwing a temper tantrum and demanding discussion she does not understand be cancelled.<br /><br />What\xe2\x80\x99s worse is that the teaching hospital caved to King\xe2\x80\x99s bullying nonsense and cancelled an educational autism event that dozens of doctors should have attended. What cowards! Then they basically apologized! \xe2\x80\x9cWe are pausing, deeply reflecting and learning before we consciously take next steps, \xe2\x80\x9c said a Sadhguru Center representative.<br /><br />Why capitulate to a historic 21 year old with, clearly, no real expertise with autism. My son cannot read, write, speak or care for himself in any way. He needs and continues to need treatment in the form of speech and occupational therapy. Like nearly half of ASD people, he also needs regular medical help for his epilepsy and IBD. This treatment is not \xe2\x80\x9cviolently ableist,\xe2\x80\x9d it is essential to his well-being.</p>\r\n\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t    <p class="entry-more-link font-entrybody"><a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/harvard-sophomore-kristin-king-rails-against-violently-ableist-sadhguru-autism-awareness-panel.html#more">Continue reading "Harvard Sophomore Kristin King Rails Against Violently Ableist Sadhguru Autism Awareness Panel" &raquo;</a></p>\n                        \n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" href="https://profile.typepad.com/rescuepost">Age of Autism</a> on May 23, 2022 at 06:00 AM in <a entry">\n\n\n\n<!-- DISPLAY FULL POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/best-of-hey-autism-awareness-whered-ya-go.html">Best Of: Hey Autism Awareness, Where\'d Ya Go?</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e20263e9a0636f200b-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="Broken blue light bulb" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e20263e9a0636f200b img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e20263e9a0636f200b-250wi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="Broken blue light bulb" /></a>Note: Cathy has today off. Did you notice how few stories there were about autism last month?&#0160; Cathy did, last year. We&#39;ve dropped off the radar in the public eye, yesterday&#39;s darling. <br /><br />###<br /><br />By Cathy Jameson</p>\r\n<p>Around this time last year, <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2020/04/mid-month-blues.html" rel="noopener" target="_blank">I noticed that autism had all but dropped off the news cycle</a>.&#0160; It appears to have taken a back seat again this year.&#0160; No big fan of how the month of April has been blue-washed for well over a decade, I\xe2\x80\x99m okay with fewer autism awareness campaigns.&#0160;</p>\r\n<p>Always a strong proponent for autism action, I\xe2\x80\x99m not even seeing that in this month\xe2\x80\x99s news stories.&#0160; <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2021/02/the-fading-flu-shot.html" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Like the flu</a>, and <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2020/10/hey-measles-whered-you-go.html" rel="noopener" target="_blank">like the measles</a>, <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2020/10/hey-measles-whered-you-go.html"></a> COVID19 has replaced illnesses, diseases, and other health conditions the world over.&#0160;</p>\r\n<p>Autism awareness may have disappeared from the media, but the autism epidemic still exists.&#0160; Some will argue that autism, a spectrum disorder, is not an epidemic.&#0160; While it\xe2\x80\x99s not a disease or illness, autism, a condition that can significantly impact physical and mental health, does fit the CDC\xe2\x80\x99s definition of epidemic. From <a href="https://www.cdc.gov/csels/dsepd/ss1978/glossary.html" rel="noopener" target="_blank">their website: CDC.gov</a></p>\r\n<p><strong><em>epidemic</em></strong><em>&#0160;the occurrence of more cases of disease, injury, or other health condition than expected in a given area or among a specific group of persons during a particular period. Usually, the cases are presumed to have a common cause or to be related to one another in some way</em></p>\r\n<p>Last updated in 2020, the current rate, which has risen steadily for decades, is 1 in 54 reported cases.&#0160; Even though the numbers are not a true representation, if that trend continues more will be added at the next reporting period.&#0160; Based on data from years ago, and from only a handful children in only a handful of states, a more accurate rate is likely much higher.&#0160; With that, I\xe2\x80\x99d say that one can absolutely use the <a href="https://tacanow.org/autism-statistics/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">word epidemic to describe what\xe2\x80\x99s happening</a>! &#0160;<a href="https://tacanow.org/autism-statistics/"></a></p>\r\n<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e2027880259890200d-pi"><img alt="Taca prevalence" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e2027880259890200d img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e2027880259890200d-400wi" style="width: 400px; display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="Taca prevalence" /></a></p>\r\n<p>&#0160;</p>\r\n<p>Regardless of how high the statistics are, autism news is scant these days.&#0160;</p>\r\n<p>When I looked for an autism-specific news story last Tuesday, a few half-hearted reports of groups \xe2\x80\x9clighting it up blue\xe2\x80\x9d could be found.&#0160; But they certainly didn\xe2\x80\x99t come with the pomp and circumstance previous April autism stories have had.&#0160; I did notice, however, that some are pushing for autism acceptance this year, not awareness. <a href="https://www.disabilityscoop.com/2021/03/23/calls-grow-for-april-to-be-designated-autism-acceptance-month/29254/"></a><a href="https://www.disabilityscoop.com/2021/03/23/calls-grow-for-april-to-be-designated-autism-acceptance-month/29254/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Acceptance?</a>&#0160; I\xe2\x80\x99d rather not.</p>\r\n\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t    <p class="entry-more-link font-entrybody"><a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/best-of-hey-autism-awareness-whered-ya-go.html#more">Continue reading "Best Of: Hey Autism Awareness, Where\'d Ya Go?" &raquo;</a></p>\n                        \n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" href="https://profile.typepad.com/rescuepost">Age of Autism</a> on May 22, 2022 at 06:00 AM in <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/cathy-jameson/">Cathy Jameson</a> </span> <span class="separator">|</span> <a class="permalink" href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/best-of-hey-autism-awareness-whered-ya-go.html">Permalink</a>\n\n \n\t<span class="separator"> | </span>\n\t\n\t\t\t <a class="entry-comments" class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/autism-and-mental-health-continue-to-vex-uk-school-system.html">Autism and Mental Health Continue to Vex UK School System</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e20278807dfaf1200d-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="Abadnonned school" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e20278807dfaf1200d img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e20278807dfaf1200d-250wi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="Abadnonned school" /></a>Note: What are schools to do with the continuing explosion of children who need special ed services?&#0160; Bey9nd school, how are families to manager short and long term.&#0160; Parents depend on their children in their golden years. What happens when the children still depend on the parents?<br /><br />By Anne Dachel<br /><br />I cannot imagine how long this can go on in the UK and Ireland. There are always increases in the number of special education students, always another new special school announced, always more money being spent. The solution is always more spending and more services, yet no one sees where this is going.</p>\r\n<p>How long can a country keep this up? What happens when massive numbers of disabled students age out of school with nowhere to go?</p>\r\n<p>Here\xe2\x80\x99s what\xe2\x80\x99s out there recently. This is the news no one is worried about.</p>\r\n<p><strong>England: </strong>The latest figures from the Department for Education are out.</p>\r\n<p><em>As of January 2022, there were 473,255 children with plans in place, compared with 430,697 the previous year, marking a 9.9 per cent increase.</em></p>\r\n<p><em>The number of children subject to EHCPs and statements, which predated the plans, has increased each year since 2010 and the latest figures indicate further dramatic rises are likely, as demand among parents for assessments is increasing.</em></p>\r\n<p><em>The figures show that requests for an assessment for a plan have rocketed by almost a quarter from 75,951 in 2020 to 93,302 in 2021. <strong>This is the highest figure since the data was first collected in 2016.</strong></em></p>\r\n<p>This was really bad news for children with severe disabilities.</p>\r\n<p><em>\xe2\x80\x9cThe latest release of pupils with high level special educational needs and disabilities (SEND) shows that the government do not have a plan to support children and young people with high level special educational needs and disabilities,&quot; said NEU joint general secretary Kevin Courtney.</em></p>\r\n<p><strong>England:</strong> An Ipswich MP introduced a bill calling for universal dyslexia screening.</p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t    <p class="entry-more-link font-entrybody"><a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/autism-and-mental-health-continue-to-vex-uk-school-system.html#more">Continue reading "Autism and Mental Health Continue to Vex UK School System" &raquo;</a></p>\n                        \n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/us-proposal-to-empower-world-health-organization-who-would-violate-nations-sovereignty-citizens-freedom.html">U.S. Proposal to Empower World Health Organization (WHO) Would Violate Nations\xe2\x80\x99 Sovereignty & Citizens\xe2\x80\x99 Freedom</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e20282e156659e200b-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="HFDF" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e20282e156659e200b img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e20282e156659e200b-250wi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="HFDF" /></a>News Provided By<br />Health Freedom Defense Fund<br /><br /><a href="https://healthfreedomdefense.org/wfd/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Read and consider signing the World Freedom Declaration HERE</a>.</p>\r\n<p>May 19, 2022, 12:00 GMT</p>\r\n<p><em>U.S. Proposal to Empower World Health Organization (WHO) Would Violate Nations\xe2\x80\x99 Sovereignty &amp; Citizens\xe2\x80\x99 Freedom</em></p>\r\n<p><strong>Even a cursory reading of the proposed amendments shows a stunning and unprecedented ceding of basic public health powers to an international body, overriding nations\xe2\x80\x99 sovereignty and citizens\xe2\x80\x99 rights\xe2\x80\x9d</strong></p>\r\n<p><em>\xe2\x80\x94 HFDF president Leslie Manookian</em></p>\r\n<p>IDAHO, UNITED STATES, May 19, 2022 /<a href="http://www.einpresswire.com" rel="noopener" target="_blank">EINPresswire.com</a>/ -- Defending individuals\xe2\x80\x99 health freedom and self-determination \xe2\x80\x93 and protecting national sovereignty \xe2\x80\x93 is the aim of the <a href="http://healthfreedomdefense.org/wfd/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">World Freedom Declaration</a> signed by 30 organizations and 33 leaders from around the globe objecting to proposed U.S. <a href="http://apps.who.int/gb/ebwha/pdf_files/WHA75/A75_18-en.pdf" rel="noopener" target="_blank">amendments</a> to the International Health Regulations. <br /><br />The amendments, offered by the U.S. Department of Health and Human Services, would empower the World Health Organization (WHO) to seize executive governance powers over member states, granting government powers to unelected and unaccountable bureaucrats \xe2\x80\x93 all in the name of combatting a future health emergency. The amendments will be considered at the 75th World Health Assembly which begins May 22, 2022. <br /><br />The agreement, unlike a formal global treaty, is not subject to approval by the U.S. Congress. <br /><br />\xe2\x80\x9cEven a cursory reading of the proposed amendments shows a stunning and unprecedented ceding of basic national public health powers to an international body, overriding nations\xe2\x80\x99 basic sovereignty and citizens\xe2\x80\x99 basic rights,\xe2\x80\x9d said Leslie Manookian, Founder and President of the Health Freedom Defense Fund (<a href="http://healthfreedomdefense.org/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">HFDF</a>), the organizer of the international declaration. \xe2\x80\x9cWe have come together to sound the alarm bell about the freedom that the Biden Administration is about to give away to the flawed World Health Organization.\xe2\x80\x9d <br /><br />The World Freedom Declaration was signed by 30 organizations and 33 advocates for health freedom from around the world, including internationally respected experts in public health, attorneys, and advocates. On May 18th, the declaration will be available to the public.</p>\r\n\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t    <p class="entry-more-link font-entrybody"><a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/us-proposal-to-empower-world-health-organization-who-would-violate-nations-sovereignty-citizens-freedom.html#more">Continue reading "U.S. Proposal to Empower World Health Organization (WHO) Would Violate Nations\xe2\x80\x99 Sovereignty & Citizens\xe2\x80\x99 Freedom" &raquo;</a></p>\n                        \n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" href="https://profile.typepad.com/rescuepost">Age of Autism</a> on fa-facebook"></i></a>\n     \n</span>\n\t</p>\n\n\n</div>\n\n\n</article>\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\n    \n\n\n\n\n<!-- entry shared -->\n\n<article class="post entry">\n\n\n\n<!-- DISPLAY FULL POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/laugh-or-cry-researchers-catch-up-with-autism-parents-25-years-later.html">Laugh or Cry: Researchers Catch Up With Autism Parents 25 Years Later</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e20282e1560057200b-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="You don&#39;t say" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e20282e1560057200b img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e20282e1560057200b-250wi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="You don&#39;t say" /></a>Decades ago, a mentor taught me a saying, &quot;Don&#39;t punish progress.&quot; It&#39;s pretty hard not to scream and shake my fists, &quot;You SHOULD have listened to Andrew Wakefield instead of running him out of town on a rail.&quot;&#0160; Don&#39;t punish progress.&#0160; If young autism parents are still paying any attention to biomedical symptoms, causes and treatments, let&#39;s hope they read <a href="https://safeminds.org/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Safeminds</a>&#39; post from Monday.<br /><br />May 15, 2022</p>\r\n<p><a href="https://safeminds.org/news/stress-anxiety-and-social-withdrawal-linked-to-gi-problems-in-children-with-autism/" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><strong>A Bidirectional Relationship Exists Between Internalizing Behaviors and Gastrointestinal Issues</strong></a></p>\r\n<p>Researchers at the University of Missouri have recently published a study that suggests a connection between gastrointestinal problems, anxiety and social withdrawal for some children with autism. While conducting their study, the authors analyzed parent reports of gastrointestinal issues and <a href="https://www.verywellmind.com/internalizing-behaviors-and-depression-1066876">internalizing behaviors</a> of 621 minors with autism. The research team used <a href="https://afni.nimh.nih.gov/pathana" rel="noopener" target="_blank">path models in a structural equation modeling framework</a> to further investigate their data. After examining the parental reports, the researchers believed the best-fitting model for this brain/gut phenomenon was a bidirectional model where internalizing behaviors (e.g., withdrawn and anxious behaviors) were associated with gastrointestinal issues (e.g., constipation, diarrhea, nausea and stomach pain). Sadly, this cycle then repeats, causing an endless loop of suffering for children experiencing both GI problems and internalizing behaviors. Co-author Brad Fergson expounds on his team\xe2\x80\x99s work, stating, \xe2\x80\x9cStress signals from the brain can alter the release of neurotransmitters like <a href="https://www.health.harvard.edu/mind-and-mood/serotonin-the-natural-mood-booster" rel="noopener" target="_blank">serotonin</a> and <a href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/articles/22610-norepinephrine-noradrenaline#:~:text=Norepinephrine%2C%20also%20called%20noradrenaline%2C%20is,muscle%20cell%20or%20gland%20cell." rel="noopener" target="_blank">norepinephrine</a> in the gut, which control <a href="https://health.ucsd.edu/specialties/gastro/areas-expertise/motility-physiology/pages/default.aspx#:~:text=Gastrointestinal%20(GI)%20motility%20refers%20to,body%20starts%20this%20complicated%20process." rel="noopener" target="_blank">gastrointestinal motility</a>, or the movement of stool through the intestines.\xe2\x80\x9d He adds, \xe2\x80\x9cStress also impacts the balance of bacteria living in the gut, called the microbiota, which can alter gastrointestinal functioning. The gut then sends signals back to the brain, and that can, in turn, lead to feelings of anxiety, depression and social withdrawal. The cycle then repeats, so novel treatments addressing signals from both the brain and the gut may provide the most benefit for some kids with gastrointestinal disorders and autism.\xe2\x80\x9d Ferguson is currently involved in a clinical trial to assess how stress-reducing medication affects gastrointestinal problems.&#0160;</p>\r\n<p><a href="https://consumer.healthday.com/b-5-3-how-stress-and-gastro-issues-combine-to-harm-kids-with-autism-2657218770.html" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Original Article</a></p>\r\n<p><a href="https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s10803-022-05539-6" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Original Study Abstract</a></p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\n\t\t\t\n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" href="https://profile.typepad.com/rescuepost">Age of Autism</a> on May 18, 2022 at 06:00 AM in <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/science/">Science</a> </span> <span class="separator">|</span> <a class="permalink" href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/laugh-or-cry-researchers-catch-up-with-autism-parents-25-years-later.html">Permalink</a>\n\n \n\t<span class="separator"> | </span>\n\t\n\t\t\t <a     </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202942fab0a86200c-pi" /></a>From Children&#39;s Health Defense - whose focus is humanity. <br /><br /><a href="https://childrenshealthdefense.org/defender/steve-kirsch-humanity-censorship-rally-rfk-jr-podcast/?itm_term=home" rel="noopener" target="_blank">RFK, Jr. to Speak at May 19 \xe2\x80\x98Humanity Against Censorship\xe2\x80\x99 Rally</a><br /><br />By Susan C. Olmstead</p>\r\n<p>As recently as a year ago, Steve Kirsch was \xe2\x80\x9ca believer\xe2\x80\x9d of what he was being told about <a href="https://childrenshealthdefense.org/defender_category/covid/">COVID-19</a> vaccines \xe2\x80\x94 in fact, the successful high-tech entrepreneur got both doses of Moderna\xe2\x80\x99s vaccine.</p>\r\n<p>But after doing his own research, Kirsch\xe2\x80\x99s viewpoint changed and he started speaking out against the vaccines \xe2\x80\x94 and that led to him being permanently banned from LinkedIn and Twitter, he told Robert F. Kennedy, Jr. on an episode of <a href="https://anchor.fm/rfkjr/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">\xe2\x80\x9cRFK Jr. The Defender Podcast.\xe2\x80\x9d</a></p>\r\n<p>Kirsch and Kennedy will speak at the \xe2\x80\x9cHumanity Against Censorship\xe2\x80\x9d <a href="http://humanityagainstcensorship.org/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">rally and demonstration</a> in Menlo Park, California, May 19 at 3 p.m. PT.</p>\r\n<p>Kirsch is executive director of the <a href="https://www.vacsafety.org/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Vaccine Safety Research Foundation</a>. He\xe2\x80\x99s also the founder of the <a href="https://www.treatearly.org/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">COVID-19 Early Treatment Fund</a>, an organization involved in researching early treatments for COVID-19.</p>\r\n\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t    <p class="entry-more-link font-entrybody"><a Menlo Park, CA" &raquo;</a></p>\n                        \n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted    \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/beyond-rainbows-and-butterflies.html">Beyond Rainbows and Butterflies</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e20282e155a6f3200b-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="7B805B30-84E2-433F-B6BF-CD9888814B30" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e20282e155a6f3200b img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e20282e155a6f3200b-250wi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="7B805B30-84E2-433F-B6BF-CD9888814B30" /></a>I saw this post circulating on Facebook yesterday, and had to share it. April was autism whatever you want to call it month. And a quiet one it was. Not as many feel good stories. A few arguments over awareness versus acceptance. Some nattering about the puzzle piece versus the infinity rainbow symbol.&#0160; <a href="https://www.drbognerhealth.com/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Dr. Bogner, of Bogner Health</a> in Bloomfield Hills, Michigan wrote the post. I was unfamiliar with Dr. Bogner. He&#39;s a functional medicine practitioner. It felt affirming to read his words in a world where autism parents are hanging on for dear life behind closed doors. Over twenty years I took Mia and Gianna to their first DAN! (RIP) doctor, a then elderly allergist named Frank Waickman, who was a colleague of Dr. Rimland. After examining Mia and Gianna, he turned to me, 36 years old, pregnant with my third baby, and said, &quot;How are YOU doing, Kim? How are you taking care of yourself.&quot; I&#39;ve never forgotten that moment of human kindness. Thank you, Dr. Bogner, for your affirmation of the struggles.<br /><br />###</p>\r\n<p>To all YOU warriors\xe2\x80\xa6</p>\r\n<p>\xe2\x80\xa6standing at your son\xe2\x80\x99s ER bed while he is restrained getting injected with antipsychotics for his rage.<br /><br />\xe2\x80\xa6kneeling next to the bathtub at 2am while he is screaming and punching his face.<br /><br />\xe2\x80\xa6screaming while he beats you in the backyard and the neighbors calling the cops.<br /><br />\xe2\x80\xa6pulling over on the expressway while he pulls your hair so hard you almost flipped your car.<br /><br />\xe2\x80\xa6pleading with the cops not to arrest him after he beat up a kid in the supermarket\xe2\x80\xa6<br /><br />\xe2\x80\xa6ready to get in the car to pick him up early from school because he is punching himself in the chest 3000 times<br /><br />\xe2\x80\xa6holding him tight at night when he is shaking in bed wondering wtf is going on.<br /><br />Hardcore autism. That\xe2\x80\x99s the life you live.</p>\r\n<p>And you keep fighting! Because you are cut from a different cloth.<br /><br />Where we go one, we go all.<br /><br />#beyondrainbowsandbutterflies</p>\r\n<p>&#0160;</p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\n\t\t\t\n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" href="https://profile.typepad.com/rescuepost">Age of Autism</a> on May 16, 2022 at 06:00 AM in <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/current_affairs/">Current Affairs</a> </span> <span class="separator">|</span> <a class="permalink" \n</span>\n\t</p>\n\n\n</div>\n\n\n</article>\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\n    \n\n\n\n\n<!-- entry shared -->\n\n<article class="post entry">\n\n\n\n<!-- DISPLAY FULL POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/thousand-steps.html">A Thousand Steps</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e2022ad38185a6200c-pi"><img alt="Journey  never stops" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e2022ad38185a6200c img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e2022ad38185a6200c-200wi" style="width: 192px; display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="Journey  never stops" /></a></p>\r\n<p>Note: Unlike bread, our incredible library of posts rarely get stale.&#0160; Cathy is taking a weekend holiday, so we present a post from December 2018.&#0160; Enjoy.<br /><br />###</p>\r\n<p>By Cathy Jameson</p>\r\n<p>Did I tell you?&#0160; He\xe2\x80\x99s sleeping through the night.&#0160;</p>\r\n<p><em>Oh, that\xe2\x80\x99s great!&#0160; </em></p>\r\n<p>He wakes up dry, too.</p>\r\n<p><em>Even better!&#0160; </em></p>\r\n<p><em>How are his mornings?&#0160; Do you get much done? </em></p>\r\n<p>Well, after I prepare his foods and feed him, he gets just a little break.&#0160; Feedings can be tricky because he\xe2\x80\x99s gotten picky about some foods.&#0160; After breakfast is over, it\xe2\x80\x99s time for therapy.</p>\r\n<p><em>Ahh, yes.&#0160; Feedings.&#0160; I remember those days.&#0160; I\xe2\x80\x99m sure he\xe2\x80\x99ll come around.&#0160; </em></p>\r\n<p><em>How many hours of therapy does he need?</em></p>\r\n<p>Actually, if he can tolerate it and won\xe2\x80\x99t need to rest midday, we\xe2\x80\x99re going to increase therapy hours after the new year.</p>\r\n<p><em>That\xe2\x80\x99s wonderful!&#0160; What are his latest milestones? Anything finally clicking? </em></p>\r\n<p>He\xe2\x80\x99s learning to communicate his wants better, and almost staying with an activity through to completion.&#0160; He\xe2\x80\x99s showing more signs that bathroom skills may be the next big thing\xe2\x80\xa6</p>\r\n<p><em>Like sitting on the toilet??</em></p>\r\n<p>Wouldn\xe2\x80\x99t that be a dream come true!&#0160;</p>\r\n<p><em>It would.&#0160; Do you think he has the motor skills for it? </em></p>\r\n<p>I do, but the big question is does he have the sensation for it.&#0160; You know, when he\xe2\x80\x99s doing something he wants to do and is really engrossed in the activity, it\xe2\x80\x99s like he can\xe2\x80\x99t even tell he\xe2\x80\x99s soiled his diaper.&#0160;</p>\r\n<p><em>I\xe2\x80\x99ve heard that before.&#0160; What else?&#0160; Any other self-help skills he\xe2\x80\x99s close to mastering? </em></p>\r\n<p>He\xe2\x80\x99s getting there\xe2\x80\xa6clearing his bowl and plate from the table, tucking in the dining room chair he just sat in, helping make his bed, putting dirty laundry in the laundry room\xe2\x80\xa6some basic, typical skills.</p>\r\n\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t    <p class="entry-more-link font-entrybody"><a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/thousand-steps.html#more">Continue reading "A Thousand Steps" &raquo;</a></p>\n                        \n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" \n</span>\n\t</p>\n\n\n</div>\n\n\n</article>\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\n    \n\n\n\n\n<!-- entry shared -->\n\n<article class="post entry">\n\n\n\n<!-- DISPLAY FULL POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/cars-upon-thars-1.html">Cars Upon Thars</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202942faa7e4a200c-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="35546432-4514-468A-9A86-31E4AE4F0828" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e202942faa7e4a200c img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e202942faa7e4a200c-250wi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="35546432-4514-468A-9A86-31E4AE4F0828" /></a></p>\r\n<p>The world is in utter turmoil. But here in the USA, where plastic straws are banned and you have to carry your e. coli strewn reusable shopping bags where ever you shop, from coast to coast, idling cars waste $4.75 a gallon gas while waiting half an hour or more for $5.75 cups of 1200 calorie beverages. Obese America. Guzzling gas and GMO beverages while paying lip service to social causes to fit in on social media.<br /><br />We are a nation of numbskulls and nitwits.<br /><br />And that&#39;s today&#39;s mood.<br /><br /><br /></p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\n\t\t\t\n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" href="https://profile.typepad.com/rescuepost">Age of Autism</a> on May 14, 2022 at 06:00 AM in <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/current_affairs/">Current Affairs</a> </span> <span <span class="separator">|</span> <span class="entry-footer-links-plusone"></span> <span class="separator">|</span> <span class="entry-footer-links-pinterest">\n     <a \n</span>\n\t</p>\n\n\n</div>\n\n\n</article>\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\n    \n\n\n\n\n<!-- entry shared -->\n\n<article class="post entry">\n\n\n\n<!-- DISPLAY FULL POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/best-of-autism-tsunami-series-by-mark-blaxill.html">Best of: Autism Tsunami Series by Mark Blaxill</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e20282e1552ee8200b-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="Nothing to see here" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e20282e1552ee8200b img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e20282e1552ee8200b-250wi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="Nothing to see here" /></a>We&#39;re approaching the second half of 2022. Another year races on, and real help for autism is at a low point. Go ahead and Google &quot;Autism,&quot; just the word. Then look at the news features. <a href="https://www.npr.org/2022/05/12/1098506522/nonspeaking-valedictorian-autism-college-commencement-speech" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Elizabeth Bonker is featured prominently</a>, which is terrific. She&#39;s the college Valedictorian who uses spelling to communicate. I will note, and I mean no disrepect to Elizabeth&#39;s success, NPR and other news outlets have written that she lost her speech at 15 months.&#0160; If she had lost her ability to walk, surely the reports would have said the reason. But regressive autism? Gloss over it and move on. The other news stories are all based on neurodiversity. I suppose we should be grateful there was not a drowning story. Mercury is in retrograde, I&#39;m told. And the world seems to be as broken as can be. I think we should revisit Mark&#39;s work. And remember our roots.&#0160; Deep and painful as they may be. <br /><br />###</p>\r\n<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e20278803cb8cb200d-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="Mark Blaxill Chilren&#39;s March" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e20278803cb8cb200d img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e20278803cb8cb200d-250wi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="Mark Blaxill Chilren&#39;s March" /></a>NOTE:&#0160; We&#39;ll have an audio file to accompany Anne&#39;s transcription.&#0160; This is part 1 of a 5 part series. Thank you.<strong><br /><br /></strong>By Anne Dachel<strong><br /><br /></strong></p>\r\n<p><a class="inline-player" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/files/mark.blaxill__2021-07-25_15-34-29.mp3">Mark Blaxill Autism Tsunami Part 1</a><strong><br /><br />Question 1: Tell us about your study, </strong><strong><em><a href="https://link.springer.com/article/10.1007/s10803-021-05120-7?fbclid=IwAR0UBTBw-qkGUCi3hK2uzarhlHH4ZuB5iho-FPXV7NpMtTG8qDnRYVq4UaI" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Autism Tsunami: the Impact of Rising Prevalence on the Societal Cost of Autism in the United States</a>.</em></strong>&#0160; What motivated you and the other authors to look into the future impact of autism?<strong>&#0160; <br /></strong></p>\r\n<p><strong>Mark: </strong><em>My motivation has been 20 years long. (Inaudible)\xe2\x80\xa6and it was pretty obvious for too long, the numbers were exploding.</em></p>\r\n<p><em>California and everywhere you looked, the numbers were going up, and that invalidated the orthodox story line. </em></p>\r\n<p><em>(Inaudible) </em>Mark dismissed the official claims of better diagnosing/diagnostic substitution.</p>\r\n<p><em>And we\xe2\x80\x99ve known that for a long time, Anne.</em></p>\r\n<p><em>I first started writing about that in 2001, 2003, in that area. I started writing in the Journal of Autism and Developmental Disorders when they started trying to blame it on diagnostic substitution.</em></p>\r\n<p><em>It was obvious that the work that they were doing \xe2\x80\xa6(inaudible) </em></p>\r\n<p><em>I wrote to them. I got some colleagues to write. \xe2\x80\xa6</em></p>\r\n<p><em>The authors that argued that it was diagnostic substitution had to retract their findings because it was obvious that they were arithmetically wrong. </em></p>\r\n<p><em>The rate of autism was going up, and the rate of intellectual disability was not declining. </em></p>\r\n<p><em>Then I wrote a paper that was published in 2004, <strong><a href="https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/15504445/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">What\xe2\x80\x99s going on? The question of time trends in autism</a>.</strong> </em></p>\r\n<p><em>I argued that the rates were going up and it was real, all over the world, particularly in the United States and the UK. </em></p>\r\n<p><em>I know you focus very heavily on the United States and the UK both of which have rates that are going up. </em></p>\r\n<p><em>And then I kept writing about it. </em></p>\r\n<p><em>I wrote a book called <strong><a href="https://www.amazon.com/Age-Autism-Medicine-Man-Made-Epidemic/dp/B0055X6B9G" rel="noopener" target="_blank">The Age of Autism</a>.</strong> </em><a href="https://www.amazon.com/Age-Autism-Medicine-Man-Made-Epidemic/dp/B0055X6B9G"></a></p>\r\n<p><em>I wrote another book called <strong><a href="https://www.amazon.com/Denial-Refusing-Epidemic-Children-Families/dp/1510716947" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Denial</a>,</strong> </em><em>both with Dan Olmsted. </em></p>\r\n<p><em>One in 2010 and another in 2017. </em></p>\r\n<p><em>You\xe2\x80\x99re kind of screaming at the universe, please pay attention. This is a crisis.</em></p>\r\n<p><em>Anne, you do this every day. I do this in longer cycle projects. We\xe2\x80\x99re doing much of the same work. </em></p>\r\n\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t    <p class="entry-more-link font-entrybody"><a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/best-of-autism-tsunami-series-by-mark-blaxill.html#more">Continue reading "Best of: Autism Tsunami Series by Mark Blaxill" &raquo;</a></p>\n                        \n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/flip-the-script.html">Flip The Script</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e20278807c705e200d-pi"><img alt="143C1FC7-7F7D-498C-BE1D-9D1901F8F59C" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e20278807c705e200d img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e20278807c705e200d-400wi" style="width: 400px; display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" title="143C1FC7-7F7D-498C-BE1D-9D1901F8F59C" /></a></p>\r\n<p>Note: Please visit <a href="https://millionsagainstmandates.org/" rel="noopener" target="_blank" title="">Millions Against Medical Mandates</a></p>\r\n<p>###</p>\r\n<p><br />I posted the above Tweet yesterday, and then posted it on Facebook with a caveat. Caveat means warning.&#0160; It read: &quot;<em>Boobies! We set our snark meter to stun on this one.</em> Followed by, <em>Mandate breastfeeding to ease the formula shortage. Medically exempt moms can buy formula. Medical exemptions will only be granted by La Leche League, not your own Dr. It&#39;s for the health of babies. Don&#39;t complain</em>.&quot;&#0160; And.... madness ensued in the comments.&#0160;</p>\r\n<p>Most readers got it - the irony. Others not so much.&#0160; I&#39;m not taking a stance pro or con breastfeeding. I&#0160; have three kids who had both. My Mom made formula for my brother with a Karo syrup recipe in 1970. I&#39;m fully aware not every Mom can breastfeed - for reasons personal to her. <br /><br />The nation would go into an uproar if breastfeeding was &quot;mandated&quot; to stretch the limited supply of formula for those who could not breastfeed. You know, for the greater good of babies. And yet, we just came off of a year and a half where men and women, Moms and Dads lost their jobs, were banned from all aspects of society and ostracized with glee across social and mainstream media for their Covid vaccination choice.&#0160; So I wrote a quick Tweet that was meant to point out how crappy medical mandates are.&#0160; All of them. <br /><br />If one person sees that vaccine mandates are just as intrusive as my imaginary Tweet topic was, it was worth losing some Facebook followers. <br /><br />Silence is submission. I won&#39;t be silent.</p>\r\n<p>&#0160;</p>\r\n<p>&#0160;</p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\n\t\t\t\n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" href="https://profile.typepad.com/rescuepost">Age of Autism</a> on May 12, 2022 at 06:00 AM in <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/current_affairs/">Current Affairs</a> </span> <span class="separator">|</span> <a class="permalink" href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/flip-the-script.html">Permalink</a>\n\n \n\t<span class="separator"> | </span>\n\t\n\t\t\t <a class="entry-comments" href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/flip-the-script.html#comments">Comments (8)</a>\n\t\n\n\n          </p>\n\n\n          <!-- technorati tags -->\n\n\n\n          <!-- post footer links class="icon fab fa-pinterest"></i></a>\n\n</span> <span class="separator">|</span> <span class="entry-footer-links-facebook_like">\n     \n     <a href="https://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.ageofautism.com%2F2022%2F05%2Fflip-the-script.html" target="_blank"><i class="icon fab fa-facebook"></i></a>\n     \n</span>\n\t</p>\n\n\n</div>\n\n\n</article>\n \n\n\n\n\n\n\n    \n\n\n\n\n<!-- entry shared -->\n\n<article class="post entry">\n\n\n\n<!-- DISPLAY FULL POSTS-->\n\n     \n\n       <h2 class="entry-header font-entryheader">\n           \n        <span class="entry-title">\n<a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/us-fda-lowers-the-efficacy-bar-for-covid-vaccine-eua-for-toddlers-to-6.html">US FDA Lowers The Efficacy Bar for Covid Vaccine EUA for Toddlers to 6</a>\n        </span>\n       </h2>\n\n\n\n\n\n\t\t\t<div class="entry-body font-entrybody">\n\t\t\t\t<p><a class="asset-img-link" href="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e20278807c4650200d-pi" style="float: left;"><img alt="Covid toddler" class="asset  asset-image at-xid-6a00d8357f3f2969e20278807c4650200d img-responsive" src="https://www.rescuepost.com/.a/6a00d8357f3f2969e20278807c4650200d-250wi" style="width: 250px; margin: 0px 5px 5px 0px;" title="Covid toddler" /></a>Head shaking report at Children&#39;s Health Defense regarding the Emergency Use Authorization Pfizer and Moderna so desperately seek, as a gateway to landing on the CDC Pediatric vaccine schedule, which means guaranteed customers from 2 to eternity.&#0160; Can you imagine lowering the bar for efficacy, and subjecting toddlers to a vaccine that could be virtually ineffective yet have all of the risk?&#0160; And parents will cheer for the ability to dose their kids, thinking they are protecting them. Remember how that felt, so many years ago? I do.<br /><br />###</p>\r\n<p><a href="https://childrenshealthdefense.org/defender/covid-vaccines-kids-efficacy-standard-fda/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">COVID Vaccines for Kids Under 6 Won\xe2\x80\x99t Have to Meet 50% Efficacy Standard, FDA Official Says</a></p>\r\n<p>The U.S. Food and Drug Administration\xe2\x80\x99s (FDA) top vaccine official <a href="https://endpts.com/fdas-peter-marks-to-congress-youngest-kids-vaccine-wont-need-to-hit-50-efficacy-mark/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">told a congressional committee</a> on Friday that COVID-19 vaccines for kids under 6 will not have to meet the agency\xe2\x80\x99s 50% efficacy threshold <a href="https://www.fda.gov/media/142749/download" rel="noopener" target="_blank">required</a> to obtain Emergency Use Authorization (EUA).</p>\r\n<p>The FDA is reviewing data from Moderna\xe2\x80\x99s two-shot vaccine for infants and toddlers 6 months to 2 years old, and for children 2 to 6 years old.</p>\r\n<p>The agency is awaiting data on Pfizer and BioNTech\xe2\x80\x99s three-dose regimen for children under age 5 after two doses of its pediatric vaccine <a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/health/2021/12/17/pfizer-vaccine-young-children-third-shot/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">failed</a> to trigger an immune response in 2-, 3- and 4-year-olds comparable to the response generated in teens and adults.</p>\r\n<p>According to <a href="https://endpts.com/fdas-peter-marks-to-congress-youngest-kids-vaccine-wont-need-to-hit-50-efficacy-mark/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Endpoints News</a>, Dr. Peter Marks, director of the Center for Biologics Evaluation and Research at the FDA, told the House Select Subcommittee on the Coronavirus Crisis the agency would not withhold authorization of a pediatric vaccine if it fails to meet the agency\xe2\x80\x99s 50% efficacy threshold for blocking symptomatic infections.</p>\r\n<p><a href="https://childrenshealthdefense.org/defender_category/covid/">COVID-19</a> vaccines for adolescents, teens and adults had to meet the requirement.</p>\r\n<p>\xe2\x80\x9cIf these vaccines seem to be mirroring efficacy in adults and just seem to be less effective against <a href="https://childrenshealthdefense.org/defender/pfizer-shot-teens-less-effective-omicron-study/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Omicron</a> like they are for adults, we will probably still authorize,\xe2\x80\x9d Marks said.&#0160; Read more at <a href="https://childrenshealthdefense.org/defender/covid-vaccines-kids-efficacy-standard-fda/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">COVID Vaccines for Kids Under 6 Won\xe2\x80\x99t Have to Meet 50% Efficacy Standard, FDA Official Says</a></p>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\n\n\t\t\t\n\n\n\n\n\n<hr />\n\n\n<div class="entry-footer">\n          <p class="entry-footer-info font-entryfooter"><span class="post-footers">Posted by <a rel="author" href="https://profile.typepad.com/rescuepost">Age of Autism</a> on May 11, 2022 at 05:00 AM in <a href="https://www.ageofautism.com/vaccines/">Vaccine Safety</a> </span> <span class="separator">|</span> <a class="permalink" href="https://www.ageofautism.com/2022/05/us-fda-lowers-the-efficacy-bar-for-covid-vaccine-eua-for-toddlers-to-6.html">Permalink</a>\n\n \n\t<span class="separator"> | </span>\n\t\n\t\t\t <a
